#Author:Varadattasuta
#Text:Śāṅkhāyanaśrautasūtrabhāṣya
#Comments:Śāṅkhāyanaśrautasūtra
#Edition:Hillebrandt; re-edition Meharchand Lachhmandas Publications 1981
#Data entry:Oliver Hellwig



1.1.1.[1]	puruṣasyābhimataphaladāyī jagadutpattibījaṃ yajñaḥ /
1.1.1.[2]	yadyapi ca dravyadevatātyāgātmā tathāpyatra sāṅgo vivakṣitaḥ /
1.1.1.[3]	idamatra pradhānametānyaṅgāni iyamitikartavyatā /
1.1.1.[4]	evaṃ sādhyasādhanarūpeṇa maryādayā śrutisiddhayā prathayiṣyāmaḥ /
1.1.1.[5]	gurāvātmani ca bahuvacanaṃ śiṣṭaiḥ smaryate /
1.1.1.[6]	tatra codayanti yajñamiti dvitīyā na prāpnoti /
1.1.1.[7]	avayavaṣaṣṭhyā tu bhavitavyam /
1.1.1.[8]	akṛtsnatvāt /
1.1.1.[9]	tadayuktam /
1.1.1.[10]	kutaḥ /
1.1.1.[11]	śruteḥ /
1.1.1.[12]	sa eṣa sarvakāmasya yajñaḥ /
1.1.1.[13]	sa eṣa svargakāmasya yajña iti /
1.1.1.[14]	tasmādadoṣaḥ /
1.1.1.[15]	yajñamityekavacanaṃ jātyapekṣam /
1.1.1.[16]	adhikārasūtrametat /
1.1.1.[17]	pratijñā ca śiṣyabuddhisamādhānārthā /
1.1.2.[1]	yajñamiti dvitīyāntaṃ prakṛtamiha prathamayā vipariṇamyate /
1.1.2.[2]	tadarthaḥ sa iti nirdeśaḥ /
1.1.2.[3]	sa yajñastrayāṇāṃ varṇanāṃ bhavatīti vākyaśeṣaḥ /
1.1.2.[4]	athavā sacchabdaḥ sādhuvācī pūrvapadam /
1.1.2.[5]	trayāṇāmityuttarapadam /
1.1.2.[6]	tenaitaduktaṃ bhavati /
1.1.2.[7]	śobhanānāṃ trayāṇāṃ varṇānāṃ yajñe 'dhikāraḥ /
1.1.2.[8]	tadevamaṅgahīnāśrotriyaṣaṇḍhaśūdravarjaṃ adhikāraḥ siddho bhavati /
1.1.2.[9]	kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ arthinaḥ samarthāśca śudrāḥ pratilomāśca nādhikriyante /
1.1.2.[10]	ucyate /
1.1.2.[11]	śrutidarśanāt /
1.1.2.[12]	ayajñiyānvā etadyajñena prasṛjati śūdrāṃstvaditi śatapathe /
1.1.3.[1]	brāhmaṇaśca kṣatriyaśca brāhmaṇakṣatriyau /
1.1.3.[2]	tayoryaḥ śūdryāṃ jātaḥ putrastasyāvarṇatvānna prāpnoti /
1.1.3.[3]	vaiśyasya ca yaḥ karaṇyāmutpadyate tasya ca na prāpnoti /
1.1.3.[4]	tadarthaṃ vacanam /
1.1.4.[1]	saṃyogaḥ saṃbandhaḥ idamasyeti viśeṣanirdeśaḥ /
1.1.4.[2]	tamakṛtvā yadvidhīyate tatsādhāraṇaṃ bhavati /
1.1.4.[3]	[ye tatra prakṛtāḥ] /
1.1.4.[4]	paribhāṣāsūtrametannyāyaprāptam /
1.1.4.[5]	atrodāharaṇam /
1.1.4.[6]	darśapūrṇamāsau trayāṇāṃ varṇānām /
1.1.4.[7]	anvāhāryaścaturṇāmṛtvijām /
1.1.5.[1]	saṃyogo 'sādhāraṇyena vyapadeśaḥ /
1.1.5.[2]	tena hetunā saṃyujyāpyucyamānaṃ vyavatiṣṭhate /
1.1.5.[3]	vyavasthitaviṣayaṃ bhavati /
1.1.5.[4]	ārthaścātra saṃyogo 'bhipreto na śābdaḥ /
1.1.5.[5]	tadyathā /
1.1.5.[6]	purodhākāmayajño brāhmaṇasya /
1.1.5.[7]	somāṅgamagnicayanaṃ dīkṣāsaṃyogāt /
1.1.6.[1]	viśiṣṭasaṃniveśaḥ śarīrasthasūtro yajñopavītī śiṣṭaprasiddhaḥ /
1.1.6.[2]	tathā ca manuḥ /
1.1.6.[3]	uddhṛte dakṣiṇe pāṇāvupavītyucyate budhaḥ /
1.1.6.[4]	savye prācīnamāvītī nivītī kaṇṭhasajjane //
1.1.6.[5]	īdṛśo yajñopavītī devārthāni karmāṇi haviḥprakṣepaprabhṛtīni tadaṅgāni cetthaṃbhūtaḥ karoti /
1.1.6.[6]	kutaḥ /
1.1.6.[7]	upavītaṃ devānāmupavyayate devalakṣmameva tatkuruta iti vacanāt /
1.1.7.[1]	prācīnāpavītī kṛtāpasavya ityarthaḥ /
1.1.7.[2]	pitṛṇāmimāni pitryāṇi /
1.1.7.[3]	piṇḍapitṛyajñaśrāddhādīni /
1.1.7.[4]	tāni prācīnāpavītī kuryāt /
1.1.7.[5]	karmagrahaṇamanuvartate /
1.1.7.[6]	tenodīratāmiti śaṃsane na prācīnāvītī /
1.1.7.[7]	kartṛdharmaścāyaṃ /
1.1.7.[8]	prāṅnyāyānītyatra karmadharmaḥ /
1.1.7.[9]	tena sarvasādhanānāṃ dakṣiṇācāratā /
1.1.7.[10]	ato yogabhedenoktam /
1.1.8.[1]	yenādhikaraṇenahotrādinā saṃyujyeta saṃbadhyeta tenācamanaprabhṛti /
1.1.8.[2]	nānyathā /
1.1.8.[3]	tena ca saṃyuktaḥ pravṛttakarmā na vyāvarteta /
1.1.8.[4]	vyāvartanaṃ bhramaṇaṃ tanna kuryāt /
1.1.8.[5]	tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ /
1.1.8.[6]	vivṛtyāvṛtya vetarathāvṛttiḥ /
1.1.9.[1]	yajñaṃ yajñāntareṇa vicchindati ha vā etadyajñamiti śrutyantarāt /
1.1.9.[2]	athavā tadadhikaraṇaṃ hautrādi padārthāntareṇa na vyaveyāt /
1.1.9.[3]	na ca vyavadadhyāt /
1.1.9.[4]	caśabdādgārhapatyāhavanīyau ca /
1.1.10.[1]	yajñopavītyādikā āvṛtāṃ lakṣaṇā /
1.1.10.[2]	āvṛcchabdena karmāṇyabhidhīyante /
1.1.10.[3]	lakṣaṇā prāyovṛttirityarthaḥ /
1.1.10.[4]	keṣāṃcicoddeśa iti sūtracchedaḥ /
1.1.10.[5]	teṣāmapyayamevārthaḥ /
1.1.11.[1]	ityāvṛtāmiti vartate /
1.1.11.[2]	uddiśyate padyate /
1.1.11.[3]	āmnāya ityeko 'rthaḥ /
1.1.11.[4]	ya uddeśaḥ pāṭhakramo brāhmaṇe sūtre vā tenaiva krameṇāvṛtaḥ kartavyāḥ /
1.1.11.[5]	na tu ṛtūnāṃ pāṭhakrameṇānuṣṭhānaṃ sarvasvāraparākayormadhye pāṭhāt /
1.1.12.[1]	yajñādhikārī 'nuvartate /
1.1.12.[2]	yajñe sarvatra avacane uttarata upācāraḥ /
1.1.12.[3]	upācāro 'nuṣṭhānam /
1.1.12.[4]	uttarataupācāro vai yajña iti śruteḥ /
1.1.12.[5]	kvacidvacane 'pi svasya dhiṣṇyasya paścādupaviśet /
1.1.12.[6]	samīpe upa āṅprayogāt na dūre /
1.1.13.[1]	prāgityapyayaṃ dikśabdaḥ /
1.1.13.[2]	nyāyaśabdo dharmaparyāyaḥ /
1.1.13.[3]	ācāraparyāyo vā /
1.1.13.[4]	yatra devārthāni karmāṇi tatra prāgeva /
1.1.13.[5]	karmaṇi prācī digaṅgīkartavyā /
1.1.14.[1]	pitṛṇāmamūni pitaro vā devatā yeṣāṃ tāni dakṣiṇācāreṇa kartavyāni /
1.1.15.[1]	āsīna upaviṣṭaḥ /
1.1.15.[2]	nyāyaśabda uktaḥ /
1.1.15.[3]	bāhvṛcyaṃ bahvṛcāmnāyoktam /
1.1.15.[4]	tadupaviṣṭena kartavyam /
1.1.16.[1]	tiṣṭhannanvāhāgnimanthanīyā ityevamādiṣu vacaneṣu vikalpo mā bhūditi sūtrārambhaḥ paribhāṣāṇāmanityatājāpanārtham /
1.1.16.[2]	tena tathā ca śākhāntarīyo hotrāsamāsaḥ /
1.1.17.[1]	yadanādiṣṭakartṛkaṃ bāhvṛcyaṃ taddhotā kuryāt /
1.1.17.[2]	cakāro bāhvṛcyānukarṣaṇārthaḥ /
1.1.17.[3]	vacanavirodhābhyāṃ maitrāvaruṇādayo'pi kuryuḥ /
1.1.17.[4]	sapta hotāra ṛtuśo yajantīti hotṛśabdaprayogāt /
1.1.18.[1]	prabhṛtiśabda ādivacanaḥ /
1.1.18.[2]	trisaṅkhyāmārabhya ye ṛggaṇā ṛksamudāyāsteṣāṃ prathamāyāmuttamāyāṃ ca triruktiḥ pratyekaṃ kartavyā /
1.1.18.[3]	kiṃ sarvatra /
1.1.18.[4]	netyucyate /
1.1.18.[5]	anyatra japebhyaḥ /
1.1.18.[6]	japānvarjayitvetyarthaḥ /
1.1.18.[7]	triprabhṛtiṣviti gaṇaviśeṣaṇaṃ kurvannetajjñāpayati /
1.1.18.[8]	kvaciddhi ko 'pi gaṇo'sti /
1.1.18.[9]	kimetasya jñāpane prayojanam /
1.1.18.[10]	vartate paśugaṇe manoteti paśudvaye 'pi manotāyā āvṛttiḥ siddhā bhavati /
1.1.19.[1]	atra okāra ādeśa vidhīyate /
1.1.19.[2]	sa ca deśatvātsthānamapekṣate /
1.1.19.[3]	taducyate /
1.1.19.[4]	svarāṇāmṛci saṃniviṣṭānāṃ yo 'nyaḥ svarastadādeḥ sthāne vidhīyate /
1.1.19.[5]	tatra kadācidṛgante svaraḥ kevalo bhavati /
1.1.19.[6]	kadācitsavyañjanaḥ /
1.1.19.[7]	sa cobhayarūpo 'pi cchandomānamityucyate /
1.1.19.[8]	tasya yadādau vyañjamaṃ tattadaṅgameva /
1.1.19.[9]	tasmātparamokārasya sthānam /
1.1.19.[10]	atastasminbhavati /
1.1.19.[11]	sa ca śuddhaḥ apṛkta ityarthaḥ /
1.1.19.[12]	caśabdātkvaciduttamādṛgakṣarāt /
1.1.19.[13]	tatrodāharaṇam /
1.1.19.[14]	upāṃśuyājo bhavati /
1.1.19.[15]	bhavataṃ dāśuṣe mayaḥ /
1.1.19.[16]	omiti /
1.1.19.[17]	tacca vakṣyamāṇena sūtreṇa /
1.1.19.[18]	uttamasya chandomānasyodāharaṇam /
1.1.19.[19]	jinvatomiti /
1.1.19.[20]	kecittu cakāramṛggaṇārthamityevaṃ vyācakṣate /
1.1.20.[1]	ya okāraḥ pūrvasūtre sthānī vihitaḥ sa makārānto bhavati /
1.1.20.[2]	omiti /
1.1.21.[1]	taṃ śuddhaṃ makārāntaṃ ca praṇava ityācakṣate yājñikāḥ /
1.1.21.[2]	praṇavaprayojanaṃ sapraṇavo dvitīyaścaturthaśceti /
1.1.21.[3]	kecittu uttamasya ca cchandomānasyetyata ārabhya taṃ praṇava ityācakṣata ityevamantamekaṃ sūtraṃ praṇavasaṃjñārthaṃ varṇayanti /
1.1.21.[4]	tadapyupapadyata eva /
1.1.22.[1]	avasānaṃ virāmaḥ /
1.1.22.[2]	tasminnavasāne makārāntaṃ praṇavaṃ kuryāt sarveṣu ṛggaṇeṣu /
1.1.22.[3]	tadyathā /
1.1.22.[4]	sveṣu kṣayeṣu vājinom /
1.1.22.[5]	sarvagrahaṇātkṛtrimagaṇeṣvapi /
1.1.22.[6]	tadyathā /
1.1.22.[7]	uśantastvetyekāṃ sāmidhenīṃ triranūcya /
1.1.22.[8]	atrāpi sarvagrahaṇādgaṇadharmalakṣaṇaḥ śuddhaḥ praṇavaḥ siddho bhavati /
1.1.22.[9]	sapuronuvākyeṣviti bahuvrīhisamāsaḥ /
1.1.22.[10]	tena saheti tulyayoga iti vopasarjanasyeti ca sahaśabdasya sabhāvaḥ /
1.1.22.[11]	tenaitaduktaṃ bhavati /
1.1.22.[12]	puronuvākyāsu cāyaṃ makārāntaḥ /
1.1.22.[13]	tataḥ śaṃyorvāke na bhavati /
1.1.22.[14]	nanu puronuvākyāsu ceti ca vaktavyaṃ sukhāvabodhārtham /
1.1.22.[15]	satyam /
1.1.22.[16]	kiṃtu aprādhānyārthaṃ ca /
1.1.22.[17]	tasmātpuronuvākyānāmanyo gaṇadharmo na bhavati /
1.1.22.[18]	ataśca ṣaṣṭhe 'hani aindravāyavasya caturṇāṃ gaṇatve 'pi satyapi prathamottamayostrirvacanaṃ na bhavati /
1.1.22.[19]	makārāntaśca praṇavaḥ pratyṛcaṃ bhavati /
1.1.23.[1]	teneti vyavahitaḥ śuddhaḥ parigṛhyate /
1.1.23.[2]	tena śuddhenottarasyā ṛcaḥ pādamardharcaṃ vā yathāvacanaṃ saṃdhāyāvasyati prayoktā /
1.1.23.[3]	tatsaṃtatamityācakṣate /
1.1.23.[4]	rūḍhā hi tasyaiva saṃjñetyarthaḥ /
1.1.23.[5]	saṃtatamitītikaraṇaḥ pradarśanārthaḥ /
1.1.23.[6]	tena sahitaṃ ceti /
1.1.23.[7]	tathā ca śrutiḥ /
1.1.23.[8]	śuddha eva praṇavaḥ syācchastrānuvacanayormadhya iti ha smāha kauṣītakistathā saṃhitaṃ bhavatīti /
1.1.24.[1]	yo'yaṃ pūrva ukto dharmastriprabhṛtiṣvityevamādiṣu sa sarveṣāmṛggaṇānāṃ vyavahitānāmapi śoṃsāvo ityanena bhavati /
1.1.24.[2]	ye karmasaṃyogena codyante /
1.1.24.[3]	havirdhānapravartanādayaśca /
1.1.24.[4]	na tu japānāmakriyāsaṃyogāt /
1.1.25.[1]	vidūreṣvantarhiteṣu ca apiśabdādanantarhiteṣu ca karmasvadhvaryvādibhiḥ kriyamāṇeṣu gaṇamadhye 'ntareṇa prathamāmṛcaṃ paridhānīyāṃ cottamāmṛcaṃ saṃtānārthaḥ kartā ardharcena karaṇabhūtenākāṅkṣati /
1.1.25.[2]	tatkamādhvaryvādibhiḥ kriyamāṇaṃ pratīkṣata ityarthaḥ /
1.1.25.[3]	tadyathā /
1.1.25.[4]	jātāyānubrūhīti /
1.1.25.[5]	vidūre udāharaṇam /
1.1.25.[6]	tadyathā /
1.1.25.[7]	samānajātīyānusamaye 'ñjanīyāyāstṛtīye vacane prathame yūpe ardharcāvasānaṃ kṛtvā tata evaṃ itareṣu yūpeṣu ardharcamardharcamañjanīyāyā uktvā tato yadūrdhvastiṣṭhā draviṇeha dhattādyadā kṣayo māturasyā upastho3 ucchrayasva vanaspate samiddhasya śrayamāṇaḥ purastāt jāto jāyata ūrdhva ū ṣu ṇa ūrdhvo naḥ pāhyaṃhaso ni ketunā viśvaṃ samatriṇaṃ daha /
1.1.25.[8]	yadūrdhvastiṣṭhā ityevamādi pratiyūpamuccāryaṃ /
1.1.26.[1]	ardharcāvasānanyāyā ardharcanyāvā evaṃdhārmikā ityarthaḥ /
1.1.26.[2]	yāḥ kṛtrimā rātriparyāyastotriyānurūpādyāstadarthaḥ sūtrārambhaḥ /
1.1.26.[3]	tatra abhyāsamātrā codanā /
1.1.26.[4]	nāvasānacodanā /
1.1.26.[5]	nanu yadyevamarthaṃ sūtraṃ kathaṃ bṛhatīṃ śastvottamaṃ pādaṃ pratyādāyottarasyāḥ prathamenāvasāyeti /
1.1.26.[6]	sa doṣaḥ /
1.1.26.[7]	udāharaṇaprapañcārthatvādasyeti /
1.1.26.[8]	cakāraḥ pūrveṇa saha samuccayārthaḥ /
1.1.27.[1]	ardharcanyāvādyadanyattadvacanādbhavati /
1.1.27.[2]	trīṇi padāni samasya paṅktīnāmavasthedityayaṃ vidhiḥ kathaṃ nāma prātaranuvāka eva bhavedevamarthaṃ sūtram /
1.1.27.[3]	nanu ca kva cānyatra prāpnoti /
1.1.27.[4]	ucyate /
1.1.27.[5]	asya sūtrakārasya śīlireṣā /
1.1.27.[6]	ādye hi dṛṣṭo yo dharmaḥ sa sarvatra prāpnoti iti /
1.1.27.[7]	tadyathā /
1.1.27.[8]	tṛṇanirasane apa upaspṛśyetyuktvānyatropaspṛśyetyāha nāngrahaṇaṃ karoti /
1.1.28.[1]	uccairuccāraṇanyāyaḥ /
1.1.28.[2]	ko 'sau /
1.1.28.[3]	ṛgvedaḥ /
1.1.28.[4]	cakāro 'nyatra japebhya ityasyānukarṣaṇārthaḥ /
1.1.28.[5]	ata etaduktaṃ bhavati /
1.1.28.[6]	yajñe apavarjamṛgveda uccairbhavatīti /
1.1.28.[7]	ataśca ṛgvedavihitaṃ yajurūhapravaranāmadheyādi sarvamuccairbhavatīti /
1.1.29.[1]	upāṃśu gārhapatye patnīsaṃyājaiścarantītyatra vikalpo na bhavati /
1.1.29.[2]	bhāvapratyayanirdeśācchrutivihitaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ draṣṭavyam /
1.1.29.[3]	yathaivaivaṃ mithaḥ saṃśṛṇvīranniti /
1.1.30.[1]	samityekībhāvamācaṣṭe /
1.1.30.[2]	svāraḥ sthānam /
1.1.30.[3]	ekaṃ sthānaṃ mandrādi kāryam /
1.1.30.[4]	śabdānāṃ dhvanīnāmityarthaḥ /
1.1.30.[5]	nyāyatetivacanātprayoktuḥ svaśaktyupekṣam /
1.1.30.[6]	caśabdo 'nyatra japebhya ityasyānukarṣaṇārthaḥ /
1.1.31.[1]	yajña ityanuvartate /
1.1.31.[2]	aikasvaryamekaśrutiprayogaḥ kāryaḥ /
1.1.31.[3]	bhāvapratyayanirdeśo lakṣaṇāntaraprāpaṇārthaḥ /
1.1.31.[4]	tenājapanyūṅkhasāmasviti siddhaṃ bhavati /
1.1.31.[5]	cakāraḥ śabdānāmityasyānukarṣaṇārthaḥ /
1.1.31.[6]	pṛthagyogakaraṇāt pūrvasūtre yo vidhiḥ sa vikalpena bhavatīti vijñāyate /
1.1.32.[1]	tarāmitīṣadarthe /
1.1.32.[2]	praṇavādīnāmuccaireva vidhānāt /
1.1.33.[1]	punaḥpraṇavavacanādetallabhyate /
1.1.33.[2]	praiṣavyavahite ca /
1.1.33.[3]	śastrāntīyācca praṇavāduccaistarāṃ yājyā bhavati /
1.1.34.[1]	yāvyāyā uccaistarāṃ vaṣaṭkāraḥ kartavyaḥ /
1.1.35.[1]	yājyayā vā samo vaṣaṭkāraḥ /
1.1.35.[2]	uccaistarāṃ veti vikalpaḥ /
1.1.36.[1]	praṇavādayaḥ prasiddhāḥ /
1.1.36.[2]	saṃpraiṣagrahaṇaṃ sāhacaryārtham /
1.1.36.[3]	yatra saṃpraiṣa uccaistatra praṇavādayo 'pi /
1.1.36.[4]	ato na patnīsaṃyājādiṣu /
1.1.36.[5]	tatra sarvopāṃśutvameva vidhānāt /
1.1.36.[6]	upāṃśuhaviryāgacodanāsvityarthaḥ /
1.1.37.[1]	upāṃśuhaviḥṣviti vartate /

1.3.0.[3]	tatrāgnyādheyapunarādheyayoḥ kaṃprapadyāderaṅgajātasyāpaṭhitatvādagnyādheyapūrvatvāccāgnihotrahomasya kramaṃ bhittvā tṛtīyādhyāyaparipaṭhitau darśapūrṇamāsau śrutikrameṇaivāha /
1.3.1.[1]	vakṣyati patnīyajamānau vratyamaśnīyatāmityādi /
1.3.1.[2]	tatpūrvedyuḥ kṛtvā tataḥ paurṇamāsena haviṣā yajate yajamānaḥ /
1.3.1.[3]	haviṣeti jātyapekṣamekavacanam /
1.3.1.[4]	yadanena haviṣāśāsta iti darśanāt /
1.3.1.[5]	yaddarśapūrṇamāsayorupavasati na ha vā avratasya devā haviraśnantīti śruteḥ /
1.3.1.[6]	yadyapi śrutāvādhānakarma pūrvamuktaṃ tathāpi paurṇamāsaṃ prathamāyai tantraṃ bhavatyāmāvāsyaṃ dvitīyāyā ityanena darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ prāthamyaṃ darśitam /
1.3.1.[7]	ataḥ sūtrakāreṇa darśapūrṇamāsau prathamaṃ sūtritau /
1.3.2.[1]	upoṣya yajata ityarthaḥ /
1.3.2.[2]	dvayorapi darśapūrṇamāsayoreka evopavāso mā bhūditi pṛthaksūtram /
1.3.3.[1]	dve eveti niyamārtha ārambhaḥ /
1.3.3.[2]	ato 'nayoreva pūrvottarayorupadeśo na jyotiṣāmayanoktayoḥ /
1.3.3.[3]	cāturmāsyeṣu cādīkṣitāyanadākṣāyaṇayājinastithitrayaṃ prāpnoti /
1.3.3.[4]	sāṃnāyyasya hi dvyahakālatvāt /
1.3.3.[5]	tatra hi saṃsthitāyāṃ paurṇamāsamiti vacanāttatrāpi kathaṃ nāma dve eva paurṇamāsyau syātāmiti niyamaḥ /
1.3.3.[6]	atastatra pūrvasyāmaindraśca dohaḥ payasyā dohaya /
1.3.3.[7]	anyathā samāpte vaiśvadeve syāt /
1.3.4.[1]	dve eva vakṣyamāṇe /
1.3.5.[1]	yāṃ tithimupavasato 'stamayasamīpe pūrṇaścandramā udiyāt /
1.3.5.[2]	utsarpet /
1.3.5.[3]	yāṃ copavasato 'stamitamātra āditye candramā utsarpet /
1.3.5.[4]	te paurṇamāsyau veditavye /
1.3.5.[5]	kaiścitsūtrakāraiḥ tithitrayaṃ paurṇamāsīsaṃjñakamuddiṣṭam /
1.3.5.[6]	jyotiṣāmayane ca saṃvādādayaṃ lakṣaṇoddeśaḥ kṛtaḥ śrutiliṅgāt /
1.3.5.[7]	paryastamayamastamita iti ādityaviśeṣaṇam /
1.3.5.[8]	kutaḥ /
1.3.5.[9]	lokaprasiddheḥ /
1.3.5.[10]	pūrṇa iti candramaso viśeṣaṇamanyasyāvyabhicārāt /
1.3.6.[1]	śvaḥ anantare āgāminyahorātre na draṣṭā iti /
1.3.6.[2]	evaṃ syānmataṃ kenacitpramāṇena /
1.3.6.[3]	bhaviṣyadanadyatane /
1.3.6.[4]	yadi candro na bhavitā /
1.3.6.[5]	yasmiṃścāhani vartamāne 'darśanaṃ candramasaḥ saṃbhāvyate te amāvāsye ityucyete /
1.3.7.[1]	tatra tasmin pūrṇamāsīdvaye amāvāsyādvaye ca ijyāyāṃ kartavyāyāṃ kālaṃ prati yathākāmī svecchayā kartā syāt /
1.3.7.[2]	nanu ca paurṇamāsīdvayopadeśāt amāvāsyādvayopadeśādyajata iti vacanātkarturyāgakāla prati svecchā siddhaiva /
1.3.7.[3]	kiṃ sūtrārambheṇa /
1.3.7.[4]	ucyate /
1.3.7.[5]	anārabhyamāṇe sūtre pakṣāntepakṣānte dvedve iṣṭī prāpnutaḥ kālasyopasthitatvādyathāpratimāsam /
1.3.8.[1]	vakṣyati vyākhyātau darśapūrṇamāsau prakṛtiriṣṭipaśubandhānāmiti /
1.3.8.[2]	tatra na jñāyate ke darśadharmāḥ ke paurṇamāsadharmā iti /
1.3.8.[3]	āvāhanādayaśca śabdāḥ sādhāraṇyena paṭhitāḥ /
1.3.8.[4]	teṣāṃ cārṣamāmnānaṃ mantrāṇāṃ prakṛtāviti yathāpaṭhitānāṃ prayogaḥ prāpnoti /
1.3.8.[5]	tadvivekārthamidamārabhyate /
1.3.8.[6]	havirgrahaṇamihānuvartate /
1.3.8.[7]	kva prakṛtaṃ haviṣā yajata iti /
1.3.8.[8]	tatra tṛtīyaikavacanāntaṃ iha prathamābahuvacanena vipariṇamyate /
1.3.8.[9]	vakṣyati /
1.3.8.[10]	ubhayatrāgneyaḥ puroḍāśo 'gnīṣomīya upāṃśuyājo vaiṣṇavo vāgnīṣomīyaśca puroḍāśaḥ paurṇamāse haviṣyaindrāgno 'saṃnayato dvitīyo 'māvāsyāyāmevamādyupadeśāddhavīṃṣi vyavatiṣṭhante /
1.3.8.[11]	siddhametaduttarārthaṃ tūcyate /
1.3.9.[1]	haviḥsaṃyuktāśca ye devatāśabdā agnīṣomīyaprabhṛtayaste cāvāhanādiṣu yathopadeśaṃ bhedena prayujyanta ityarthaḥ /
1.3.9.[2]	iti paurṇamāsyāmityevamādeḥ sūtradvayasyāparo vyākhyāmārgaḥ /
1.3.9.[3]	etatpaurṇamāsyāmetadamāvāsyāyām īdṛśādupadeśādvyavatiṣṭhante /
1.3.9.[4]	asaṃkareṇa bhavantītyarthaḥ /
1.3.9.[5]	nanūpadeśātmāptaiva vyavasthā /
1.3.9.[6]	satyaṃ /
1.3.9.[7]	ucyate /
1.3.9.[8]	śābdenaiva saṃyogena vyavasthā bhavati /
1.3.9.[9]	nārthena /
1.3.9.[10]	uktā cārthenāpi vyavasthā /
1.3.9.[11]	seha neṣyate /
1.3.9.[12]	śābdenaiva vyavasthā niyamyate /
1.3.9.[13]	yadi punarārthenaiva vyavasthā syāt tato vatsāpākaraṇasaṃyogātmanāyyapakṣa eva pratyāśanaṃ prasajyeta /
1.3.9.[14]	rākāsinīvālyostu rākā paurṇamāsyāṃ syāt sinīvālī amāvāsyāyāṃ yathāsaṃkhyayogāt /
1.3.9.[15]	atastanmā bhūditi sūtrārambhaḥ /
1.3.9.[16]	śrutau ca saṃyogaḥ paṭhitaḥ /
1.3.9.[17]	sa ca vyavasthā heturbhavati /
1.3.9.[18]	tatsaṃyuktāśca śabdāḥ /
1.3.9.[19]	taditi sarvanāmnā paurṇamāsyamāvāsyayornirdeśaḥ /
1.3.9.[20]	pūrvasūtreṇa śābde saṃyoge prāpte vacanaṃ prākaraṇikasaṃyogaprāpaṇārtham /
1.3.9.[21]	paurṇamāsyamāvāsyāprakaraṇasaṃyuktāḥ kaṃprapadyādayo darśapūrṇamāsayoreva vyavatiṣṭheran nanu sarvārthā anārambhavādā iti kṛtvā tatra ko doṣaḥ syāt /
1.3.9.[22]	ucyate /
1.3.9.[23]	aprākṛtā bhaveyuḥ /
1.3.9.[24]	ataśca pratiṣedho 'rtha ityevamādibhirna nivarteran /
1.3.10.[1]	asaṃyujya vidhīyamānaṃ sādhāraṇamiti prāpte asaṃdehārthaṃ vacanam /
1.3.10.[2]	pūrvayoryogayostadapavādo mā bhūditi /
1.3.11.[1]	ubhayoḥ paurṇamāsyamāvāsyākarmaṇorāgneyo 'gnidevatākaḥ puroḍāśo bhavati /
1.3.11.[2]	ubhayatretyadhikārārtham /
1.3.11.[3]	puroḍāśagrahaṇaṃ hoturnopayujyata iti cet /
1.3.11.[4]	ucyate /
1.3.11.[5]	upayujyate /
1.3.11.[6]	yatrāgneyaḥ puroḍāśastatrāgnirmūrdhā bhuvo yajñasyeti yājyāpuronuvākyāyugalam /
1.3.11.[7]	yatra punarāgneyamājyaṃ tatra prāyaṇīyādṛṣṭam /
1.3.12.[1]	ubhayatreti vartate /
1.3.12.[2]	agnīṣomīyadevatāka upāṃśuyājasaṃjño yāgo bhavati /
1.3.12.[3]	upāṃśudharmakaḥ /
1.3.12.[4]	śrutyupadiṣṭasyāpi ājyahaviṣo 'nupadeśo pratyāśane ājyabhakṣaṇasyāpratiṣedhārthaḥ /
1.3.13.[1]	ubhayatreti vartate /
1.3.13.[2]	vāśabdo vikalpārthaḥ /
1.3.13.[3]	viṣṇudevatyo vā upāṃśayājo bhavati /
1.3.13.[4]	viṣṇurupāṃśu yaṣṭavyo 'jāmitvāyeti śākhāntarāt /
1.3.14.[1]	agnīṣomadevatyaḥ puroḍāśaḥ paurṇamāse haviṣi bhavati /
1.3.14.[2]	haviḥśabdena karma lakṣyate /
1.3.14.[3]	ataśca paurṇamāse karmaṇi bhavatītyarthaḥ /
1.3.14.[4]	caśabda uktena saha samuccayārthaḥ /
1.3.14.[5]	tatastṛtīyatvaṃ siddhaṃ bhavati /
1.3.14.[6]	paurṇamāsagrahaṇamubhayatra mā bhūt /
1.3.14.[7]	haviṣīti vacanaṃ puroḍāśasya paurṇamāsīvikāraprāpaṇārtham /
1.3.14.[8]	tataśca aindre puroḍāśe paurṇamāsīvikārasiddhiḥ /
1.3.15.[1]	aindrāgnaḥ puroḍāśaḥ asaṃnayataḥ sāṃnāyyamakurvataḥ /
1.3.15.[2]	sāṃnāyyamiti saṃskṛte dadhipayasī ucyete /
1.3.15.[3]	taddvitīyamamāvāsyāyāṃ havirvikalpena bhavati /
1.3.15.[4]	asomayājino 'pītyetasmādeva vacanāt jñāyate /
1.3.15.[5]	yasminpakṣe etanna tasminnaindrāgno dvitīyaḥ /
1.3.15.[6]	dvitīya iti trayodaśāmāvāsyāyāmāhutayo hūyanta iti carakāṇāṃ śrutirupāṃśuyājapratiṣedhārthā /
1.3.15.[7]	tatpakṣeṇa sūtritam /
1.3.16.[1]	indradevatyaṃ sāṃnāyyaṃ saṃnayataḥ sāṃnāyyena yāgaṃ kurvato dvitīyaṃ havirbhavati /
1.3.16.[2]	tadāhutīnāṃsomayājī saṃnayettada sameva nayediti śatapathe /
1.3.16.[3]	somayājī saṃnayetkāmāditara iti kātyāyanasya /
1.3.17.[1]	mahendro devatā asyeti māhendra sāṃnāyyam /
1.3.17.[2]	vāśabdo vikalpārthaḥ /
1.3.17.[3]	sarvatrātra havirupadeśo yena ca dravyeṇa yakṣyamāṇaḥ syāditi tajjātīyāśanapratiṣedhārthaḥ /
1.3.18.[1]	amāvāsyāyāmiti vartate /
1.3.18.[2]	viṣṇudevatyamupāṃśuyājaṃ kuryāt /
1.3.18.[3]	kaḥ /
1.3.18.[4]	asaṃnayan asāṃnāyyayājī /
1.3.18.[5]	atha yadasaṃnayan puroḍāśāvantareṇopāṃśvājyasya yajatīti śrutatvāt /
1.3.18.[6]	tuśabdo 'tra vyavasthitavikalpārthaḥ /
1.3.18.[7]	tenāmāvāsyāyāṃ sāṃnāyyayājino 'gnīṣomau /
1.3.18.[8]	asāṃnāyyayājino viṣṇuriti /
1.3.18.[9]	evametāni pradhānānyuktāni /
1.3.18.[10]	keṣāṃcicchākhināṃ prāksomayāgādekapuroḍāśā paurṇamāsī /
1.3.18.[11]	tatrāpyupāṃśuyājo 'styeva /
1.3.18.[12]	tacca sūtrakārāḥ prāyeṇa ca sūtrayanti /
1.3.18.[13]	utpannānuṣṭhānatvāt /
1.3.18.[14]	utpannānuṣṭhānaṃ ca na kartavyam /
1.3.18.[15]	mahāvrate liṅgadarśanāt /
1.3.18.[16]	tadetatpurāṇamutsannaṃ na kāryamiti /
5.1.0.[1]	uktāni prāgaiṣṭikāni karmāṇi saumikāni karmāṇi /
5.1.0.[2]	somasyāvasaraḥ /
5.1.0.[3]	tadarthamāha /
5.1.1.[1]	śrutādhyayanagrahaṇadhāraṇaśrautasmārtakarmānuṣṭhānavanto brāhmaṇā ṛṣaya ihocyante /
5.1.1.[2]	kutaḥ /
5.1.1.[3]	ko na ṛṣirbhaviṣyatīti ta etānanūcānānapaśyanniti niruktadarśanāt /
5.1.1.[4]	śatapathaśruteśca /
5.1.1.[5]	yo vai jñāto 'nūcānaḥ sa ṛṣiriti/ teṣāṃ putrā ārṣeyāstānyūnastaruṇānanūcānānadhyayanavyākhyānakṣamānṛtvijo yajñakṛto vṛṇīte /
5.1.1.[6]	yajñavyāpārāyābhiprasādayatītyarthaḥ /
5.1.1.[7]	somena yakṣyamāṇaḥ /
5.1.1.[8]	somena yakṣya ityabhi pravṛttaḥ /
5.1.1.[9]	/
5.1.2.[1]	caturo mahartvijo vṛṇīte /
5.1.2.[2]	sarvān vā sadasyasaptadaśān /
5.1.2.[3]	ubhayaṃ śākhāntarāt /
5.1.3.[1]	candramā me daivo brahmā etadupāṃśu /
5.1.3.[2]	tvaṃ mānuṣa etaduccairbrūyāt /
5.1.3.[3]	evaṃ brahmāṇaṃ vṛṇīte mantraliṅgāt /
5.1.4.[1]	evaṃ sarvān vakṣyamāṇānṛtviṅnāmāntaṃ mantramupāṃśūktvā śeṣamuccairiti /
5.1.5.[1]	udgātāraṃ vṛṇīte mantravarṇāt /
5.1.5.[2]	nau daiva iti dviyajamānake /
5.1.5.[3]	no deva iti bahuyajamānake /
5.1.5.[4]	evaṃ sarveṣu varaṇamantreṣu pūrveṣu cottareṣu ca /
5.1.6.[1]	anena mantreṇa hotāraṃ vṛṇīte mantravarṇādityuktam /
5.1.7.[1]	vāyurma ityevamādinā mantreṇadhvaryuṃ vṛṇīte /
5.1.8.[1]	prajāpatirma ityevamādinā mantreṇa sadasyasaṃjñakaṃ vṛṇīte /
5.1.8.[2]	prajāpatirnau deva iti diyajamānake/ no deva iti bahuyajamānake /
5.1.8.[3]	ayamupadraṣṭā bhavati /
5.1.8.[4]	sarpatsu na śūnyaṃ sadaskuryāditi chandogānām /
5.1.9.[1]	ṛtavo ma ityevamādinā mantreṇa hotrāśaṃsino vṛṇīte /
5.1.9.[2]	hotrakā hotrāśaṃsina ucyante /
5.1.10.[1]	bhargaṃ ma ityevamādikaṃ mantraṃ vṛta ṛtvik japitvānantaraṃ japātpṛcchati yadi pūrvaṃ na jñāto yo 'yaṃ yajñaḥ kartavyaḥ /
5.1.10.[2]	kimayamahīna uta neti /
5.1.10.[3]	kaccicchabdaḥ kiṃśabdasyārthe /
5.1.10.[4]	anudeśyaḥ sa ucyate yaḥ kṛtvānyasmai jīvate mṛtāya vā anudiśyate /
5.1.10.[5]	yathā kātyāyanenoktam /
5.1.10.[6]	ukhāṃ cedbibhranmriyeta sopakaraṇamāhitāgnyāvṛtā dagdhvā nediṣṭhyagniṃ citvā tamasmā anudiśedityeka iti /
5.1.10.[7]	nyastārtvijyastu nyastaṃ parityaktamārtvijyaṃ yasminnanyena kenacidyajamānasya doṣeṇa /
5.1.10.[8]	nītāsu dakṣiṇāsu yaḥ śeṣaḥ sa nītadakṣiṇo yajñaśeṣaḥ /
5.1.10.[9]	evaṃ dṛṣṭādṛṣṭadoṣaparihārārtham /
5.1.10.[10]	yadyeteṣāmanyatamo na bhavati tataḥ pratiśṛṇoti /
5.1.10.[11]	itarathā pratyācaṣṭe /
5.1.10.[12]	pratiśravaḥ kriyābhyupagamaḥ /
5.1.10.[13]	pratyākhyānaṃ tadviparyayaḥ /
5.2.1.[1]	ṛtvigvaraṇādanantaraṃ devayajanajoṣaṇam /
5.2.1.[2]	mahartvijo yajamānaśca prākpravaṇaṃ devayajanaṃ joṣayeran /
5.2.1.[3]	śākhāntarāt /
5.2.2.[1]	pūrvottarayordiśoryadantarālaṃ tadavanataṃ devayajanaṃ yajñakāmasya kuryāt /
5.2.3.[1]	yasmindevayajane sthito hotā sāmidhenyādyanubruvannāhavanīyamādityamapaśca nadītaḍāgādiṣvavasthitāḥ paśyettadbrahmavarcasakāmasya devayajanaṃ bhavati /
5.2.4.[1]	śuddhapakṣe dīkṣāprakramaḥ /
5.2.4.[2]	puṣye nakṣatre puṣyādau samāpanaṃ ca somasya /
5.3.1.[1]	aparāhṇe dīkṣaṇīyāsaṃjñakā agnāviṣṇudevatākā iṣṭirbhavati /
5.3.1.[2]	saṃjñākaraṇaṃ trihaviśca dīkṣaṇīyetyevamādyartham /
5.3.2.[1]	niyamārthaṃ vacanam /
5.3.2.[2]	pūrvakārivaśāddhavirantare 'pi /
5.3.3.[1]	pañcadaśa sāmidhenīranvāheti śruteḥ /
5.3.4.[1]	iṣṭirviśeṣyate /
5.3.4.[2]	upāṃśahaviriyamiṣṭiryatrāpi bahūni havīṃṣi bhavanti /
5.3.5.[1]	preddho agna imo agna iti virājau sviṣṭakṛto yājyānuvākye bhavataḥ śākhāntarāt /
5.3.6.[1]	nitye vā sviṣṭakṛto yājyānuvākye bhavataḥ /
5.3.6.[2]	virājau sviṣṭakṛto veti sūtre kartavye virāṇnityayostulyatāprajñāpanārthaṃ sūtrabhedaḥ /
5.3.6.[3]	ataśca yatra yātayāmatvadoṣa āśaṅkyate tatrāviniyuktayoḥ kriyā siddhā bhavati /
5.3.7.[1]	uttarasyāṃ devayajyāyāmupahuto bhūyasi haviṣkaraṇa idaṃ me devā havirjuṣantām /
5.3.7.[2]	etā ilāyāṃ tisra āśiṣaḥ /
5.3.7.[3]	etāsāṃ sthāne'sya yajñasyāgura udṛcamaśīya ityetāni ṣaṭ padāni bhavanti /
5.3.7.[4]	upahuto 'yaṃ yajamāna ityasya prākṛtasyeha pāṭhaḥ sandhyarthaḥ /
5.3.7.[5]	itikaraṇaśca vispaṣṭārthaḥ /
5.3.7.[6]	ilāyāmukto viśeṣaḥ /
5.3.7.[7]	sūtāvāke ucyate /
5.3.7.[8]	uttarāṃ devayajyāṃ bhūyo haviṣkaraṇamāyuḥ suprajāstvaṃ divyaṃ dhāmeti pañcāśiṣo nāmagrahaṇasthānantarāḥ /
5.3.7.[9]	tāsāṃ sthāne 'sya yajñasyāgura udṛcamaśīyeti ṣaṭ padāni bhavanti /
5.3.7.[10]	tacca vakṣyamāṇasūtrābhiprāyeṇa yajamānanāmagrahaṇamutsṛjya tasmātpūrvaṃ padatrayaṃ gṛhītvā sūtrakāreṇa prayogaḥ pradarśitaḥ /
5.3.7.[11]	āśāsta iti cāvasānārthaṃ paṭhanti /
5.3.7.[12]	evaṃ vyavasthitamilāyāṃ sūktāvāke ca kuryāt /
5.3.7.[13]	prāktārtīyamavanikyāḥ puroḍāśeḍāyāḥ /
5.3.7.[14]	tṛtīyasavane bhavā tārtīyasavanikī /

5.11.6.[1]	tasmādu tatropāṃśu careyuriti śruteḥ /

5.11.7.[2]	ya ugra iva śaryaheti yājyā / 8. tvaṃ soma kratubhiḥ sukraturbhūḥ somasya puronuvākyā /
5.11.7.[3]	aṣāḍhaṃ yutsu pṛtanāsu paprimiti yājyā / 9. yaḥ pūrvyāya vedhase navīyase viṣṇoḥ puronuvākyā /
5.11.7.[4]	tamu stotāraḥ pūrvyaṃ yathā videti yājyā /
5.11.8.[1]	yāvadādiṣṭaṃ yāvaduktamityarthaḥ /
5.11.8.[2]	prākṛtasya sviṣṭakṛdādernivṛttyarthaṃ vacanam /
5.11.9.[1]	agnerya ugra iveti puronuvākyā /
5.11.9.[2]	agnirvṛtrāṇīti yājyā /
5.11.9.[3]	somasyāṣāḍhaṃ yutsviti puronuvākyā /
5.11.9.[4]	tvaṃ soma kratubhiriti yājyā /
5.11.9.[5]	viṣṇostamu stotāraḥ pūrvyamiti puronuvākyā /
5.11.9.[6]	yaḥ pūrvyāyeti yājyā /
5.11.9.[7]	evamāparāhṇike upasañcaraṇe viparyāsaḥ /
5.11.9.[8]	evamiyamiṣṭidvayenaikopasadgaṇyate /
5.11.9.[9]	itare apyevameva draṣṭavye /
5.11.10.[1]	imāṃ me agne samidhamityetāstisraḥ sāmidhenīrdvitīye 'hani paurvāhṇika upasañcaraṇe 'nubrūyāt /
5.11.11.[1]	dvitīya evāhanyaparāhṇe upasadyāya mīlhuṣa ityetāstisraḥ sāmidhenīranubrūyāt /
5.11.11.[2]	śeṣaṃ hyastanavat /
5.11.12.[1]	yenaiva prakāreṇa prathame 'hanyupasattenaiva tṛtīye 'pyahani kartavyā /
5.11.12.[2]	evametāstisra upasadaḥ svaśrutau /
5.11.12.[3]	śrutyantare tu jyotiṣṭoma eva dvādaśāpyāmnātāstatra kimayameva triko daṇḍakalitavat caturāvartata uta svasthānavṛddhyā dvādaśasaṃkhyāpūraṇamiti saṃśaya āha /
5.11.13.[1]	yā prathame 'hani sā caturahaṃ kriyate /
5.11.13.[2]	yā dvitīye sāpyevameva caturaham /
5.11.13.[3]	yā tṛtīye sā caturahamiti /
5.11.13.[4]	evametāḥ svakālāḥ svasthānasthā eva vivardherannevaṃ kramo na bādhito bhavati /
5.11.13.[5]	tuśabdaḥ saṃśayavyudāsārthaḥ /
5.11.14.[1]	pratyahaṃ vā viparyāsaṃ kuryāt /
5.11.14.[2]	yadyupasado vivardheran evamapi śrutatvāt /
5.11.14.[3]	kecittu śrutimanyārthāṃ manyamānāḥ pūrvapakṣametadicchanti /
5.11.14.[4]	siddhāntasūtraṃ tu pūrvam /
5.11.15.[1]	śvobhāvinyāṃ sutyāyāṃ yadahastadupavasathaśabdavācyam /
5.11.15.[2]	tasminprātarubhe paurvāhṇikamupasañcaraṇamāparāhṇikaṃ ca samāpya /
5.11.15.[3]	tato 'nyatkarma /
5.12.1.[1]	agnipraṇayanaṃ cāturmāsyeṣūktaṃ tadihopavasathe 'hani bhavati /
5.12.1.[2]	pravargyarahite yajñe /
5.12.2.[1]	upavasathe prātaḥ sapravargyaṃ yajñe pravargyopasadau samasya mahāvīrapātrodvāsanaṃ bhavati /
5.12.3.[1]	tatra mahāvīrapātrodvāsane prastotā sāmagānaṃ karoti /
5.12.3.[2]	kiṃ tataḥ /
5.12.4.[1]	tatra tasminprastotuḥ sāmagāne hoturapi nidhanopāyaḥ /
5.12.4.[2]	sāmanidhanopagamanaṃ paṭhanaṃ hoturapi bhavati /
5.12.4.[3]	hotṛvacanaṃ brahmādinivṛttyartham /
5.12.4.[4]	tatra prastotā sāma gāyati tatra hoturnidhanopāya iti sūtradvayakaraṇaṃ sautye 'hani pravargyapakṣe tatraiva pravargyotsādanaṃ tatrāpi hoturnidhanopāya iti jñāpanārtham /
5.12.5.[1]	nanu bhraṣṭāvasaratvādapravargye ca vidhānānna prāpnoti /
5.12.5.[2]	ucyate /
5.12.5.[3]	śrutāvaviśeṣeṇa vyākhyātam /
5.12.5.[4]	brahma vā agnistadyadupavasathe 'gniṃ praṇayantīti /
5.12.5.[5]	tatpravargyotsādanādūrdhvamupavasathe yathā syāditi sūtrārambhaḥ /
5.12.5.[6]	yeṣāmapi sautye 'hani mahāvīrapātrodvāsanaṃ teṣāmapyupavasatha evāgnipraṇayanam /
5.12.5.[7]	vyākhyātavacanāt /
5.13.1.[1]	śrutikrameṇāgnipraṇayanādanantaraṃ havirdhānapravartanamāha /
5.13.1.[2]	havirdhānapravartanamiti vakṣyamāṇasya karmaṇo nāmadheyam /
5.13.1.[3]	tadarthamāmantrito āhūto hotā yatkaroti taducyate /
5.13.2.[1]	haviḥ somākhyaṃ dhīyate 'vasthāpyata iti /
5.13.2.[2]	havirdhāne śakaṭe ucyete /
5.13.2.[3]	te prācī śālāmagreṇādhvaryuṇāvasthāpite tayordakṣiṇasyottaraṃ varmottarasya ca dakṣiṇamantareṇa tiṣṭhan hotā havirdhānābhyāṃ pravartyamānābhyāmanubrūhīti saṃpreṣitaḥ /
5.13.2.[4]	kiṃ karotītyata āha /
5.13.3.[1]	apeto janyamityevamādinā mantreṇa loṣṭaṃ prakṣipet /
5.13.3.[2]	katham /
5.13.3.[3]	dakṣiṇapādāgratalena pratīcīṃ diśaṃ prati /
5.13.4.[1]	pretāṃ yajñasya śaṃbhuveti tiṣṭhannanubrūyāt /
5.13.4.[2]	āsīnanyāyapratiṣedhārthaṃ punastiṣṭhadvacanam /
5.13.5.[1]	dyāvā naḥ pṛthivī imaṃ tayoriddhṛtavatpayaḥ /
5.13.5.[2]	yame iva yatamāne yadaitam /
5.13.5.[3]	etāstisro dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasyottaraṃ varmopasaṃlagno 'nusaṃyan anubrūyāt /
5.13.5.[4]	sa prācyaṃ dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasyottaraṃ varmopaniśrayeteti śruteḥ /
5.13.6.[1]	adhi dvayoradadhā ukthyaṃ vaca ityetāmanubrūyāt chadiṣi kīlādāvupari dīyamāne /
5.13.7.[1]	viśvā rūpāṇi pratimuñcate kavirityetāmanubrūyāt /
5.13.7.[2]	pariśrīyamāṇayoḥ rajjubhirbadhyamānayorhavirdhānayoḥ /
5.13.8.[1]	nābhiryasminphalake tannabhyam /
5.13.8.[2]	tatsthayorhavirdhānayorā vāmupasthamadruhetyetāmanubrūyāt/ yadaine nabhyasthe kuryurathā vāmupasyamadruheti śruteḥ /
5.13.9.[1]	kecidadhvaryavo nabhyasthakarma pūrvaṃ kurvanti /
5.13.9.[2]	tato madhyamasya chadiṣa āropaṇam /
5.13.9.[3]	tatra karmaviparyāse 'dhvaryuvaśādyathākarma /
5.13.9.[4]	ā vāmupasthaṃ pūrvādhi dvayorityuttarā /
5.13.10.[1]	pari tvā girvaṇo gira ityetayā paridhāya parisamāpyānuvacanaṃ tato 'nyatkarma /
5.13.11.[1]	yatra sthitenānuvacanasya prathamoktā tatra sthitvā utsṛjyate vyavāyavāgyamanabhramaṇādiniyamāt /
5.13.11.[2]	yatra tiṣṭhantatsthitvetyanuvādapareṇa sthānavidhānamato nāsīnanyāyaḥ /
5.14.1.[1]	śrutikrameṇāgnīṣomapraṇayanaṃ vaktavyam /
5.14.1.[2]	tasya tāvadavadhimāha /
5.14.1.[3]	miteṣu niṣpāditeṣu /
5.14.1.[4]	yajñāgāreṣu sadohavirdhānāgnīdhreṣu agnīṣomau praṇayanti /
5.14.1.[5]	tatrāgnimāgnīdhīyaṃ praṇayanti /
5.14.1.[6]	somaṃ havirdhānam /
5.14.1.[7]	tataḥ kimityata āha /
5.14.2.[1]	tatprabhṛtītyagnīṣomapraṇayanaprabhṛtītyarthaḥ /
5.14.2.[2]	ānūbandhyāyāḥ saṃsthānāt /
5.14.2.[3]	vakṣyati /
5.14.2.[4]	maitrāvaruṇī ca vaśānubandhyeti /
5.14.2.[5]	ā tadīyavyāpāraparisamāpteḥ /
5.14.2.[6]	antareṇa madhye cālālotkarau tīrthaṃ praveśa ityarthaḥ /
5.14.3.[1]	karma kuryāditi vākyaśeṣaḥ /
5.14.4.[1]	uttareṇāgnīdhrīyaṃ dhiṣṇyaṃ āgnīdhraśaraṇasthamagniṃ sadaścottareṇa gatvā tataḥ /
5.14.5.[1]	adhvaryuśca pratiprasthātā cādhvaryū /
5.14.5.[2]	tāvuttareṇa yajñapātrāṇi cāntaḥpātyadeśasthāni tāni cottareṇa gatvā /
5.14.5.[3]	pūrvayā dvārā śālāṃ praviśya /
5.14.5.[4]	ayaṃ yajñasaṃcaraḥ sūtrāntare prasiddhaḥ /
5.14.5.[5]	tatpratipattyarthamavyavāyodāharaṇaprapañcārthaṃ coktam /
5.14.6.[1]	śālāmukhe bhavaḥ śālāmukhīyo 'gnistasya paścādupaviśya saṃpraiṣamapekṣata iti śeṣaḥ /
5.14.7.[1]	iti kāryāntare /
5.14.7.[2]	tena kadācidadhvaryuvaśādagnaye prahriyamāṇāyānubrūhi somāya prahriyamāṇāyeti veti /
5.14.8.[1]	etāmevāsīnaḥ śeṣamanuvacanasya tiṣṭhan /
5.14.9.[1]	uttiṣṭha brahmaṇaspata iti liṅgāduttiṣṭhatsu /
5.14.10.[1]	praitu brahmaṇaspatirityetāṃ pravrajatsu liṅgādeva /
5.14.11.[1]	hotā devo amartya ityayaṃ tṛcaḥ /
5.14.11.[2]	upa tvāgne divediva iti tṛcaḥ /
5.14.11.[3]	etau tṛcāvanusaṃyannanubrūyāt liṅgānnyāyācca /
5.14.12.[1]	hotā devo amartya ityasya tṛcasya tṛtīyāyāmṛci bhūtānāṃ garbhamā dadha iti yaḥ pādastaṃ bruvan garbhakāmāyai patnyai garbhamiyaṃ labhatāmiti dhyāyāduttareṇa sado 'nusaṃyan /
5.14.12.[2]	udaraṃ vai sada iti sāmānyāt /
5.14.13.[1]	āgnīdhrīyaśaraṇe 'dhvaryavo 'gniṃ nidadhati sthāpayantītyarthaḥ /
5.14.13.[2]	ataḥprabhṛtyāgnīdhrīye prāyaścittamādhvaryavaṃ yathā syāditi sūtrārambhaḥ /
5.14.14.[1]	agne juṣasva prati harya tadvaca ityetāmāgnīdhrīya āhutau hūyamānāyāmanubrūyāt /
5.14.14.[2]	tāṃ saṃpratyetāmanubrūyāt /
5.14.14.[3]	agne juṣasva prati harya tadvaca iti tasyā evaiṣā yājyetyarthavādādāhutigrahaṇācca tadāvṛttāvāvṛttiḥ /
5.14.14.[4]	
5.14.15.[1]	uttareṇāgnīdhrīyamagniṃ anusaṃyan /
5.14.15.[2]	somo jigāti gātuvidityetāstisro 'nubrūyāt /
5.14.16.[1]	upa priyaṃ panipnatamityāhavanīye hūyamānāyāmāhutāvanubrūyāt /
5.14.16.[2]	asyāmapyāhutireva prayojikā /
5.14.16.[3]	arthavādāt /
5.14.17.[1]	tamasya rājā varuṇastamaśvineti havirdhānaṃ prapādyamāne some 'nubrūyāt /
5.14.17.[2]	vrajaṃ ca viṣṇuḥ sakhivāṁ aporṇuta ityetad bruvan gotrapadaṃ gṛhṇīyāditi vṛddhavārttā /
5.14.18.[1]	antaśca prāgā aditirbhavāsītyanubruvannanuprapadya tato 'nyatkuryāt /
5.14.19.[1]	dakṣiṇe 'nasi kṛṣṇājinamāstīrya tasmin somaṃ nidadhātītyādhvaryave nivṛtte śyeno na yoniṃ sadanaṃ dhiyā kṛtam /
5.14.19.[2]	gaṇānāṃ tvā gaṇapatiṃ havāmahe /
5.14.19.[3]	astabhnād dyāmasuro viśvavedā ityetā uttarato dakṣiṇasyānaso dakṣiṇāmukhastiṣṭhannanubrūyāt /
5.14.20.[1]	evā vandasva varuṇaṃ bṛhantamityāśīrvatyā paridhātīti śruteḥ /
5.14.21.[1]	savyāvṛddhavirdhānayoryadāgāraṃ tasya pūrvasyāṃ dvāri /
5.14.21.[2]	praveśaniṣkāśāvirodhena bahirupavibhatīti /
5.14.21.[3]	vināpi karmaṇehopaveśanavidhirayam /
5.14.22.[1]	yadyaparayā dvārādhvaryubhiḥ somaḥ prapādyate tatastenaiva hotānusamiyānna brahmayajamānau hotṛvacanāt /
5.14.23.[1]	prapādyamāne 'nuprapadyetyevamādyaparayāpi dvārā prapādyamāne pūrveṇaiva tulyam /
5.14.24.[1]	dakṣiṇena bāhunā āvṛto dakṣiṇāvṛt /
5.14.24.[2]	tādṛśo 'parayā dvārā niṣkramya tataḥ savyāvṛtsannuttareṇa havirdhāne havirdhānaśakaṭopalakṣitamāgāramuttareṇa gatvā tatraiva pūrvasyāmeva dvāryupaviśati /
5.15.1.[1]	agnīṣomadevatākena paśunā śvobhāvini sautye yajate /
5.15.1.[2]	ya evāsau somasyopavasathe 'gnīṣomīyastameva tenāpnotīti liṅgāt /
5.15.1.[3]	nanvanyatropavasathaśabdena paurṇamāsyamāvāsye ucyete /

5.15.1.[9]	satyam /

5.15.1.[12]	tathā ca nirūḍhenāyanādyantayoryajata itījyārtheṣvevāgnīṣomīyadharmā nānyeṣu /
5.15.2.[1]	yūpāyājyamānāyānubrūhītyuktaḥ añjanti tvāmadhvare devayanta ityanvāha /
5.15.3.[1]	ucchrīyamāṇāyānubrūhītyuktaḥ ucchrayasva vanaspate /
5.15.3.[2]	samiddhasya śrayamāṇaḥ purastājjāto jāyate sudinatve ahnām /
5.15.3.[3]	ūrdhva ū ṣu ṇa ūtaye /
5.15.3.[4]	ūrdhvo naḥ pāhyaṃhaso ni ketunā /
5.15.3.[5]	ityetā anubrūyāt /
5.15.4.[1]	parivīyamāṇāyānubrūhītyuktaḥ yuvā suvāsāḥ parivīta āgāditi paridhāya parisamāpyānuvacanam /
5.15.4.[2]	yūpāyājyamānāyetyevamādisaṃpreṣagrahaṇaṃ prayojakārtham /
5.15.4.[3]	atastadvaśādupaśaye 'pi yūpadharmaprāptiḥ / 5. ṛjukāyāvastho 'gnimanthanīyā anvāha /
5.15.4.[4]	tiṣṭhanniti vacanānna paścādvedeḥ /
5.15.4.[5]	anvāheti vacanāt sati manthane /
5.15.4.[6]	manthanamanvityarthaḥ /
5.15.5.[1]	yajñena yajñamayajanta devā ityetayā paridadhyāttaṃ marjayanteti sakṛduktvā /
5.15.5.[2]	etayā nvatra ca cāturmāsyeṣu cātha yatra paśurālabhyate tadetāṃ parācīmanūcya yajñena yajñamayajanta devā iti triṣṭubhā paridadhātīti śruteḥ / 7. atraiva tiṣṭhansāmidhenīranvāha /
5.15.5.[3]	manotāsūktādanantaraṃ śrutāvuktatvāt /
5.15.5.[4]	sa eva kramo mā bhūditi vacanam /
5.15.5.[5]	nanvāhutikṣapaṇārthatvādidhmasya śrutikramācca tatraivedhmādhānamanuvacanaṃ ca yuktam /
5.15.5.[6]	ucyate /
5.15.5.[7]	nedhmasya haviḥkṣapaṇārthataiva saṅkhyāniyamāt /
5.15.5.[8]	manotāsāptadaśyārthavādasaṃbandhenārthavādārthaṃ /
5.15.5.[9]	tatra śrutiḥ /
5.15.6.[1]	paśuśabdaḥ pradhānāvadānavacanam /
5.15.6.[2]	ataḥ pradhānāvadānadevatāmāvāhya avyavahitaṃ vanaspatimāvāhayet /
5.15.6.[3]	evameva śrutatvāt /
5.15.7.[1]	prakṛtivadadhvaryumāgnīdhraṃ ca saṃmṛśya ṣaṇmorvīrityevamādikaṃ mantraṃ japitvā tiṣṭhati /
5.15.8.[1]	mitrāvaruṇayorityevamādinā mantreṇa yajamāno maitrāvaruṇāya daṇḍaṃ samarpayati /
5.15.9.[1]	daṇḍaṃ pratigṛhya maitrāvaruṇo dakṣiṇāvṛddakṣiṇena hotāraṃ gatvāgrataḥ sthitaḥ pūrvo hotuḥ pratipadyate /
5.15.10.[1]	uttareṇa havirdhāne iti havirdhānāgāramuttareṇa dakṣiṇenāgnīdhrīyaṃ dhiṣṇyamadūre gatvā pūrvayā dvārā sadaḥ prapadya svasya dhiṣṇyasya paścādupaviśya maitrāvaruṇaḥ hotā tu hotṛṣadane evamanena krameṇa saṃcarapraveśanopaveśanāni kṛtvā ekādaśa vakṣyamāṇakān prayājānyajati /
5.15.10.[2]	kathamityata āha /
5.16.1.[1]	praiṣā hotā yakṣadagnimityevamādayaḥ pāśukāḥ /
5.16.1.[2]	hotā yakṣadindraṃ harivānityevamādayaśca saumikāḥ prasiddhāḥ /
5.16.1.[3]	te sarva eva maitrāvaruṇasya bhavantīti lāghavārthaṃ paribhāṣaṇam /
5.16.2.[1]	sapraiṣe ca pradāne puronuvākyā maitrāvaruṇasya bhavanti /
5.16.2.[2]	cakāraḥ pūrveṇa saha samuccayārthaḥ /
5.16.3.[1]	prayājādhikārādūrdhvam utsṛjyate maitrāvaruṇa iti yāvat /
5.16.3.[2]	yathā praiṣā maitrāvaruṇasya tathānuvacanānyapi /
5.16.3.[3]	paryagnikaraṇādīni tasyaiva bhavanti /
5.16.4.[1]	praiṣānuvākyānuvacanāni prahāṇaḥ kuvakra iva tiṣṭhandaṇḍāvambhastho maitrāvaruṇo 'nubrūyāt / 5. samidhaḥ preṣyeti viśiṣṭena saṃpraiṣeṇa saṃpreṣito hotā yakṣadagniṃ samidhā suṣamidhā samiddhamityevamādinā praiṣasūktenobhayavatā tanūnapānnarāśaṃsānyataraprayogeṇa pratyekamuttareṣu preṣyapreṣyetyukto maitrāvaruṇaḥ preṣyati /
5.16.4.[2]	praiṣānāhetyarthaḥ /
5.16.5.[1]	dāśatayīṣu daśaivāprīsūktāni /
5.16.5.[2]	teṣāṃ sāmānyaviniyogārthametatsūtram /
5.16.5.[3]	tena ghṛtaṃ mimikṣe deva tvaṣṭaryaddha cāru tvamānalityetayorviśeṣaviniyoge sati prayājata uddhāraḥ /
5.16.5.[4]	etayoḥ sthāne 'nyārṣeye kartavye /
5.16.5.[5]	yātayāmatvadoṣaparihārāyeti vṛddhasaṃpradāyaḥ / 7. yadārṣeyo yajamānastadārṣeyyā āpriyo bhavanti /
5.16.5.[6]	tadyathā /
5.16.5.[7]	vaiśvāmitrasya yajamānasya samitsamit /
5.16.5.[8]	vāsiṣṭhasya juṣasva na iti /
5.16.6.[1]	athavā samiddho adya manuṣa duroṇa ityetāḥ sarveṣāṃ bhavanti /
5.16.6.[2]	yeṣāmapi samānārṣeyamāprīsūktamasti /
5.16.6.[3]	abrāhmaṇasya tu samiddho adyetyetadeva bhavati /
5.16.6.[4]	na purohitārṣeyam /
5.16.6.[5]	pravaramātrasya tadīyasya vacanāt /
5.16.7.[1]	yastu nārāśaṃsayājī saṃbhavatsvārṣeyanārāśaṃsastasya svaiva kāryā samiddho adya manuṣa ityatrāsaṃbhavānnārāśaṃsyāḥ /
5.16.7.[2]	atrodāharaṇam /
5.16.7.[3]	ātreyasya samiddho adyeti vaikalpike prayoge narāśaṃsaḥ suṣūdatīti bhavati /
5.16.7.[4]	yeṣāṃ svā na vidyate teṣāṃ vāsiṣṭhī /
5.16.7.[5]	nirukte tathā dṛṣṭatvāt /
5.16.8.[1]	daśabhiḥ prayājaiścaritvā paryagnaye 'nubrūhītyevaṃ saṃpreṣito 'gnirhotā no adhvara ityādyāstisra ṛco 'nvāha maitrāvaruṇaḥ paribhāṣitatvāt /
5.16.9.[1]	upa preṣya hotarhavyā devebhya ityadhvaryuṇā saṃpreṣito maitrāvaruṇo 'jaidagnirasanadvājamityevamādikamupapraiṣasaṃjñakaṃ praiṣamāha /

6.1.1.[1]	agnīṣomīyeṇopavasathe paśunā yajata ityata ārabhya yaḥ paśvarthatayā karmakalāpa uktaḥ sa evānyeṣāṃ paśūnāṃ prakṛtirdraṣṭavyaḥ /
6.1.1.[2]	kutaḥ /
6.1.1.[3]	prāthamyādaṅgasākalyācca /
6.1.1.[4]	ūhayogyaṃ mantrajātaṃ prāyeṇa darśapūrṇamāsayoragnīṣomīye ca paśāvāmnātaṃ yato 'to vikṛtiṣūhacintā prastūyate /

7.4.15.[7]	kartāra ṛtvijo yajamānaścānyo'nyasmin karmavyatihāreṇopahavamanujñāmicchante /
7.4.15.[8]	prārthayanta ityarthaḥ /
7.4.15.[9]	sādhāraṇeṣu someṣvayaṃ nyāyo yujyate /
7.4.15.[10]	kadā cidbahutaraṃ pāsyāmīti /
7.4.15.[11]	asādhāraṇeṣu ca /
7.4.15.[12]	nānupahūtena somaḥ pātavya iti śruteḥ /
7.4.16.[1]	homābhiṣavakāriṇaḥ pūrvo vaṣaṭkartā bhakṣayadvacanāt /
7.4.16.[2]	tasmiṃśca sati tadviparītasya nyāyasyānavatārāt /
7.4.17.[1]	dvidevatyā aindravāyavamaitrāvaruṇāśvināḥ nārāśaṃsavantaśca grahāḥ /
7.4.17.[2]	ājyapraugamarutvatīyaniṣkevalyavaiśvadeveṣu /
7.4.17.[3]	eteṣāṃ pratibhakṣitamadhvaryuṇaikadeśaśeṣaṃ hotṛcamase 'vanayet /
7.4.17.[4]	hute tvā bhakṣitamityevamādinā mantreṇa /
7.4.18.[1]	atra śrutyantaroktaṃ dviraindravāyavaśeṣasyāvanayanam /
7.4.18.[2]	mantraśca dvirucyate /
7.4.19.[1]	avasarjanaṃ vimokaḥ /
7.4.19.[2]	sa na kartavyo dvidevatyānām /
7.4.19.[3]	yāvatsvasyasvasya śeṣasyāvanayanaṃ na kṛtamiti /
7.4.19.[4]	uktā somabhakṣaparibhāṣā /
7.4.19.[5]	idānīmavasaraprāpto dvidevatyabhakṣa ucyate /
7.5.1.[1]	iha vasurityādinā mantreṇendravāyavagrahamadhvaryave dattvānantaramupūhatau vāyurityādinā bhakṣayitvā tamevaindravāyavaṃ pragrahaṇamantreṇa punaḥ pragṛhya bhakṣamantreṇa punarbhakṣayati /
7.5.1.[2]	ūrau na niddhāti /
7.5.1.[3]	nādhvayurmuñcati nā hotā parisaṅkhyānāt /
7.5.2.[1]	adhvaryava iti vartate /
7.5.2.[2]	iha vasurityādinā mantreṇa /
7.5.2.[3]	maitrāvaruṇaṃ grahamadhvaryave pragṛhyānantaram /
7.5.3.[1]	upahūtau mitrāvaruṇāvityanena mantreṇa maitrāvaruṇaṃ grahaṃ bhakṣayati /
7.5.4.[1]	āśvinaṃ grahaṃ tamūrorādāya śiraḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ paryāṇīya avekṣya tenaiva mārgeṇa pratyānīyāvekṣate /
7.5.4.[2]	marvataḥ parihāramāśvinasya bhakṣayatīti śruteḥ /
7.5.4.[3]	avekṣaṇaṃ tu śākhāntarāt /
7.5.5.[1]	ihādhvaryave prayacchati /
7.5.5.[2]	na pūrvam /
7.5.5.[3]	āśvinavacanāt /
7.5.6.[1]	upahūtau devāvityevamādinā mantreṇāśvinaṃ bhakṣayitvānantaramupaspṛśya /
7.5.6.[2]	dvidevatyabhakṣapaddhatiratrocyate /
7.5.6.[3]	adhvarya upahyasvetyupahavamiṣṭvā tenopahūta upahūto vāyurityādinā bhakṣayet /
7.5.6.[4]	tata uro'bhimarśanamapāmupasparśanaṃ ca /
7.5.6.[5]	evaṃ yathoktamaindravāyavaṃ maitrāvaruṇamāśvinaṃ ca /
7.5.6.[6]	adhvarya upahavastasya homābhiṣavakāritvāt /
7.5.6.[7]	vaṣaṭkāranimitto hi bhakṣo dvirhi tasya vaṣaṭkarotītyaindravāyave hetvārambhāt /
7.5.7.[1]	upaspṛśyoṣṭhanilimpanādinā ilāmupahvayate /
7.5.7.[2]	ilāṅgamupasparśanam /
7.5.7.[3]	tenetarayorapi savanayorbhavati /
7.5.7.[4]	dvidevatyānāṃ prathamo bhakṣo 'thelātha hotṛcamasa iti śruteḥ /
7.5.7.[5]	upasparśanaṃ śākhāntarāt /
7.5.8.[1]	camasādhvaryavaścamasānilāsamīpamutkṣipanti /
7.5.9.[1]	hotā savyena hotṛcamasaṃ pātrīṃ ca saṃyacchatīti śruteḥ /
7.5.10.[1]	sarvatrājyalepena somasaṃsparśe varjanīyo na kevalamatra /
7.5.11.[1]	ilāmupahvayata iti prakṛtam /
7.5.11.[2]	tāmupahūya abhakṣayitvetyarthaḥ /
7.5.11.[3]	ilāyāścāyaṃ niyamaḥ /
7.5.11.[4]	tata uttarelāṃ prāśnātyeva prakṛtivat /
7.5.11.[5]	upahūyelāmavaghrāyāvasyati prāśnātyuttarelāmathāpa ācamya hotṛcamasaṃ bhakṣayatīti śruteḥ /
7.5.11.[6]	evamuttarelābhakṣācamanānantaraṃ prasthitasaṃjñakānsavanamukhīyānhotrādibhirvaṣaṭkṛtānbhakṣayanti hotrādayaḥ /
7.5.11.[7]	prātaḥsavane prasthitabhakṣe vṛddhasaṃpradāya ucyate /
7.5.11.[8]	hotā tāvadadhvarya upahyasva pratiprasthātarupahyasvetyupahavamiṣṭvā tābhyāmupūhatastejase tvā brahmavarcasāya bhakṣayāmauti bhakṣayatyayaṃ śukranimitto bhakṣaḥ /
7.5.11.[9]	bhakṣayitvā śaṃ no bhavetyanayoro 'bhidṛśya tata upaspṛśet /
7.5.11.[10]	tato 'dhvaryuṇā bhakṣite hotā pratiprasthātarupahvayasvetyupahavamiṣṭvā tenopahūtaḥ pūrvavadbhakṣoro'bhimarśanopasparśanāni kuryāt /
7.5.11.[11]	ayaṃ manthinimitto bhakṣaḥ /
7.5.11.[12]	tataḥ pratiprasthātrā bhakṣite hotā punaradhvaryū pṛṣṭvā tābhyāmupūhata unnīyamānavaṣaṭkāranimittaṃ bhakṣayatyuro'bhimarśanādi ca karoti /
7.5.11.[13]	tataḥ punarhotṛcamase samākhyānimittabhakṣārthamadhvarya upahvayasva pratiprasthātarupahyasvetyupahavamiṣṭvā tābhyāmupahūto bhakṣādi pūrvavat kuryāt /
7.5.11.[14]	tata āpyāyanaṃ yathoktam /
7.5.11.[15]	atha brahmacamasam /
7.5.11.[16]	brahmannupahyasveti tenopahūtaḥ pūrvavadbhakṣaṇādi sarvaṃ kuryādāpyāyanavarjam /
7.5.11.[17]	tata udgātṛcamasam /
7.5.11.[18]	udgātāra upahyadhvamiti upahavamiṣṭvā tairupahūtaḥ pūrvavadbhakṣaṇādi kuryāt /
7.5.11.[19]	sarvamāpyāyanavarjam /
7.5.11.[20]	na tvasyogātṛavarjaṃ bhakṣaṇaprasiddheḥ /
7.5.11.[21]	atha yajamānacamasam /
7.5.11.[22]	yajamānopahvayasva sunvannupahyasveti vopahavamiṣṭvā tenopahūtaḥ pūrvavadbhakṣaṇādi kuryāt /
7.5.11.[23]	atha maitrāvaruṇacamasam /
7.5.11.[24]	praśāstarupahvayasva adhvarya upahvayasvetyupahavamiṣṭvā tābhyāmupahūtaḥ pūrvavadbhakṣaṇadi kuryāt /
7.5.11.[25]	tato brāhmaṇacchaṃsinaścamasam /
7.5.11.[26]	brahmannupahyasvādhvarya upahvasvetyupahavamiṣṭvā tābhyāmupahūtaḥ pūrvavadbhakṣaṇādi kuryāt /
7.5.11.[27]	tataḥ potṛcamasam /
7.5.11.[28]	potarupahvayasvādhvarya upahvayasvetyupahavamiṣṭvā tābhyāmupahūtaḥ pūrvavadbhakṣaṇādi kuryāt /
7.5.11.[29]	tato neṭṛcamasam /
7.5.11.[30]	neṣṭarupahvayasvādhvarya upahvayasvetyupahavamiṣṭvā tābhyāmupahūtaḥ pūrvavadbhakṣaṇādi kuryāt /
7.5.11.[31]	tata āgnīdhracamasam /
7.5.11.[32]	agnīdupahvayasvādhvarya upahvayasvetyupahavamiṣṭvā tābhyāmupahūtaḥ pūrvavadbhakṣaṇādi kuryāt /
7.5.11.[33]	evaṃ hoturbhakṣaḥ /
7.5.11.[34]	atha brahmodgātā yajamānaśca hotarupahvayasvetyupahavamiṣṭvā tenopahūtā yathācamasaṃ hotṛvadbhakṣaṇādi kuryurāpyāyayeyuśca /
7.5.11.[35]	atha maitrāvaruṇo brāhmaṇācchaṃsī potā neṣṭāgnīdhraśca hotarupahvayasvādhvarya upahvayasvetyupahavamiṣṭvā tābhyāmupahūtāḥ svaṃsvaṃ camasaṃ hotṛvadbhakṣayeyuḥ /
7.5.11.[36]	punaśca samākhyānimittaṃ hotarupahvayasvādhvarya upahvayasvetyupahavamiṣṭvā tābhyāmupahūtāḥ svaṃsvaṃ camasaṃ hotṛvat bhakṣitaṃ bhakṣayeyurāpyāyayeyuśca /
7.5.11.[37]	iti prasthitabhakṣa uktaḥ /
7.5.11.[38]	atha prakṛtamucyate /
7.5.12.[1]	tejase tvetyādibhakṣamantraḥ prātaḥsavane autsargikaḥ /
7.5.13.[1]	ojase tvetyādimantro mādhyandine savane autsargika eva /
7.5.14.[1]	vyavasthitaḥ pratisavanamutsargaḥ /
7.5.14.[2]	vacanātprakaraṇaṃ bhittvā /
7.5.15.[1]	śaṃ no bhava hṛda ā pīta indo ityanayoro 'bhimṛśet somaṃ bhakṣayitvā /
7.5.15.[2]	bhakṣayitvetyatirekātsarvatra dvidevatyādiṣvapi /
7.5.16.[1]	etāvadāpyāyanaṃ na somāseka iti jñāpanārthaṃ yathāprāptasyopadeśasūtram /
7.5.17.[1]	ā pyāyasvetyādikā ṛgāpyāyanī /
7.5.17.[2]	tato na dravyāntaram /
7.5.17.[3]	anayā savyahastasthitasya camamasya dakṣiṇena sparśanam /
7.5.17.[4]	prātaḥsavanavacanātprātaḥsavana evānayā /
7.5.17.[5]	nottarayoḥ savanayoḥ /
7.5.17.[6]	anyathā vikalpasamuccayau syātām/
7.5.18.[1]	saṃ te payāṃsi samu yantu vājā itīyamāpyāyanī uttarayoḥ savanayoḥ /
7.5.19.[1]	hotṛbrahmodgātṛyajamānamaitrāvaruṇabrāhmaṇācchaṃsipotṛneṣṭracchāvākāgnīdhracamasāḥ savanamukhīyāḥ prasthitāḥ /
7.5.19.[2]	tānbhakṣitapratibhakṣitānnārāśaṃsārthamāpyāyayanti /
7.5.20.[1]	āpyāyanaprasaṅgamupajīvannanyatrāpyāha /
7.5.20.[2]	ājyaśastre grahabhakṣānantaraṃ ye camasāste nārāśaṃsākhyā vakṣyante /
7.5.20.[3]	tānbhakṣitapratibhakṣitānāpyāyayanti marutvatīye ca /
7.5.21.[1]	ājyādiṣu yathoddiṣṭeṣu ye vaṣaṭkāreṇa camasā havirdhānasthā eva kampyante yaduktaṃ kātyāyanena nārāśaṃsānāṃ ca kampanamiti te nārāśaṃsasaṃjñāḥ /
7.5.21.[2]	saṃvyavahārārthaṃ saṃjñākaraṇaṃ /
7.5.21.[3]	nārāśaṃsānāṃ sannānāmupavāte nārāśaṃsa iti ca /
7.5.22.[1]	devo 'sītyevamādinā nārāśaṃsānāṃ prātaḥsavane bhakṣamantraḥ /
7.5.22.[2]	prātaḥsavanavacanamuttarayoravikalpārtham /
7.5.22.[3]	nārāśaṃsavacanaṃ sahāpi grahaśeṣeṇāyameva nārāśaṃsānāṃ bhakṣamantra iti niyamārtham /
7.5.23.[1]	tasya ta ūrvaiḥ pitṛbhirityarthasaṃbandhādeva prāpnoti /
7.5.23.[2]	vikāravacanamagniṣṭuti vikārāntarapratiṣedhārtham /
7.5.24.[1]	tasya te kāvyaiḥ pitṛbhiriti tṛtīyasavane prayogaḥ /
7.6.1.[1]	akārāntasyāpyacchāvākaśabdasya sīdetiśabdena saha saṃbandhe sakārasya dvitvaṃ chāndasam /
7.6.1.[2]	śākhāntara evameva praiṣapāṭhāt /
7.6.1.[3]	atha vā /
7.6.1.[4]	acchāvākaḥ etāvatsūtramadhikārārtham /
7.6.1.[5]	anantaraṃ karma kurvannaprasūto 'pyacchāvāka ucyate yadi sīdetyaviśeṣeṇa śākhāntare praiṣaḥ /
7.6.1.[6]	vājasaneyināṃ praiṣo nāsti /
7.6.1.[7]	tatrāpyāsanamāsīnanyāyaṃ bāhvṛcyamiti paribhāṣitatvāt /
7.6.2.[1]	agreṇa sadaso bahiḥ uttareṇa adūreṇa srutiṃ śālāmukhīyādārabhya uttaravederdvāraparaṃparayā yo mārgaḥ srutiśabdena sa ucyate tamuttareṇopaviṣya /
7.6.2.[2]	kimanantaramityata āha /
7.6.3.[1]	purolāśakhaṇḍamadhvaryuṇā dattaṃ gṛhītvā tataḥ /
7.6.4.[1]	kramārthaṃ saṃpraiṣavacanam /
7.6.4.[2]	keṣāṃ cidabhyadhiko 'pi saṃpraiṣaḥ /
7.6.5.[1]	acchā vo agnimavasa ityevamādyā ṛco 'cchāvākastisro 'nvāha /
7.6.6.[1]	tisṛṇāṃ yo 'ntyo praṇavastṛtīye vacane tena saṃtataṃ vakṣyamāṇaṃ nigadamāha /
7.6.7.[1]	ayaṃ nigadaḥ /
7.6.7.[2]	etasminnacchāvākenokte /
7.6.8.[1]	sarvārtho'yaṃ madhye 'dhvaryuvacanāt dvitīya upahavamayamityādistaṃ hotarupayasveti hotrarthaḥ /
7.6.9.[1]	ayaṃ tāvatprathamaḥ kalpaḥ /
7.6.9.[2]	yadā hotā nopahvayate tadetara upahvayerannuttarasmādyatnāt /
7.6.10.[1]	nāyaṃ nigadaḥ /
7.6.10.[2]	pūrvasya nigadavacanāt /
7.6.10.[3]	tato naikasvaryaṃ noccaiṣṭvaṃ /
7.6.10.[4]	ayaṃ sunvanyajamāno agrabhīdityasya vikāreṣūhaḥ /
7.6.10.[5]	ya upahvāsyamāno bhavati sa pratyetetyevamādikaṃ mantraṃ gāva upahūtā ityevamantaṃ japitvā tata utopahūta ityaikasvaryeṇa brūyāt /
7.6.11.[1]	yaḥ punaranupahvāsyamāno bhavati sa uta no gāva upahūtā ityāto japet /
7.6.11.[2]	abhividhau cāyamāṅ draṣṭavyaḥ /
7.6.11.[3]	utopahūta iti na brūyādityarthaḥ /
7.6.11.[4]	upahvāsyamāna ucyate /
7.6.11.[5]	upahavaṃ dātumicchan /
7.6.11.[6]	tadviparīto 'nupahvāsyamānaḥ /
7.6.11.[7]	na cāyamupahavaḥ prāyaścittārtho yathā kātyāyanenoktaḥ /
7.6.11.[8]	śālāsanāsvapnau sandhivelayorvedyāṃ sutyāsvaprāyaścittamaparādha itaretarasminvopahavamiccheranyantyāmekadīkṣīti /
7.6.11.[9]	na ca kriyāviśeṣaṇārtho yathā nānupahūtena somaḥ pātavyaḥ /
7.6.11.[10]	tatropahūtaḥ /
7.6.11.[11]	ityupahavacchandogānāṃ /
7.6.11.[12]	ato'yaṃ yathoktamevaṃ kriyamāṇamabhyudayakāri bhavatīti kṛtvā kartavyaḥ /
7.6.12.[1]	utopahūta iti nokto 'cchāvāko yajamānatvenāpi sattreṣu sthito 'cchāvākavacanāt /
7.6.12.[2]	nivartadhvaṃ mānu gātetyetasya sūktasya /
7.6.12.[3]	sūktavacanāttata ārabhya vedaśeṣasya yāvacchaknuyāt prāk saṃpraiṣāttāva danudravet /
7.6.12.[4]	yāvatīriti śruteḥ /
7.6.12.[5]	prakrāntāyā ṛcaḥ samāpanam /
7.6.12.[6]	anudravediti vacanānna gaṇadharmo naikasvaryam /
7.6.13.[1]	hotā vānyatamo vā yajamānādīnāṃ arocamānamacchāvākaṃ pratyupahūya nivartadhvamiti yathoktaṃ kuryāt /
7.7.1.[1]	unnīyamānāyānubrūhītyevamadhvaryuṇā saṃpreṣitaḥ pratyasmai pipīṣata ityetatsūktamanvāha caturṛcam /
7.7.1.[2]	svayamacchāvākaḥ saptamīmiti pakṣāntaraśruteḥ /
7.7.1.[3]	sūktavacanaṃ svābhipretasidhyartham /
7.7.1.[4]	acchāvākavacanaṃ maitrāvaruṇanivṛttyartham /
7.7.2.[1]	prātaryāvabhirā gatamityaindrāgnyā yajatīti śruteḥ /
7.7.3.[1]	pūrvaprasṛptasyācchāvākīyāṃ kurvataḥ samākhyābhakṣo na prāpnoti /
7.7.3.[2]	tadarthaṃ bhakṣitavacanam /
7.7.3.[3]	aprasthitatvādāpyāyanaṃ na prāpnoti /
7.7.3.[4]	tadarthamāpyāyitavacanam /
7.7.3.[5]	adhvaryave pradāyeti nārāśaṃsasādanārtham /
7.7.3.[6]	tathā ca kātyāyanaḥ /
7.7.3.[7]	hotṛcamasavatsarvamityāha /
7.7.3.[8]	dakṣiṇāvṛdityādi niyamārtham /
7.7.3.[9]	sadovacanaṃ divaspṛṣṭhamityādikriyārtham /
7.7.3.[10]	svasya dhiṣṇyasya paścādupaviśya nirgatya purolāśaṃ prāpnoti /
7.7.3.[11]	ucchiṣṭadoṣaparihārārthaṃ nirgamanam /
7.7.4.[1]	pūrvaprasṛptā maitrāvaruṇādayaḥ /
7.7.4.[2]	teṣāmanyatamo yadi śrutyantarīyāddhotrāsamāsavacanādacchāvākīyāṃ kuryāt tataḥ svena visaṃsthitasaṃcareṇa sadaso niṣkramyācchāvākasya bahiṣkarmācchāvākasmīdetyukto 'greṇa sada ityādikaṃ kṛtvā svakarma kurute /
7.7.4.[3]	purolāśaprāśanaṃ kuruta ityayaṃ kramaḥ /
7.7.4.[4]	ke citpūrvagrahaṇādyo 'cchāvākātpūrvaḥ prasṛptaḥ karoti /
7.7.4.[5]	itarastu grāvastudaprasṛptaḥ /
7.7.4.[6]	apūrvatvāt /
7.7.4.[7]	so 'cchāvākasaṃcareṇaiva pratipadyate /
7.7.4.[8]	acchāvākīyāvacanātsakalām /
7.7.4.[9]	na bahiṣkarmamātram /
7.7.4.[10]	pūrvaprasṛpto'pi na yajamāno na sadasyo visaṃsthitasaṃcareṇetyārambhāt /
7.7.4.[11]	pratyaggamane hi sa visaṃsthitasaṃcaro na tu prāggamane /
7.7.4.[12]	sakṛddhiṣṇyopasthānam /
7.7.4.[13]	acchāvākasya bahiḥkarmeti niyamāt /
7.7.4.[14]	prasaṅgemānyatrāpi hotrāsamāse ye viśeṣāsta ucyante /
7.7.4.[15]	hotrāsamāsaśabdaśca tantrāntare prasiddhaḥ /
7.7.4.[16]	ekasya karturanekārtvijyakriyāyoge /
7.7.4.[17]	tatra saṃcarāṇāṃ sakṛtkriyā /
7.7.4.[18]	gantavyasya pradhānatvāt /
7.7.4.[19]	ilābhakṣaṇamāgnīdhre /
7.7.4.[20]	dadhibhakṣaṇaṃ daśarātre /
7.7.4.[21]	śākhāntaroktaṃ madhvaśanaṃ ghṛtasya vā /
7.7.4.[22]	tathā ṛtvigbhyastaṃ kārayediti paśubhakṣaṇam /

7.10.12.[1]	āhūya daivyāvadhvaryū ityevamādikāṃ purorucaṃ śastvā tato 'śvinā yajvarīriṣa ityetāstisraḥ śaṃset /

7.10.14.[1]	āhūya viśvāndevānityevamādikāṃ purorucaṃ ṣaṭpadāṃ śastvā tata omāmañcarṣaṇīdhṛta ityetāstisraḥ śaṃset /
7.10.15.[1]	āhūya vācāmahamityevamādikāṃ purorucaṃ pakṣe śastvā tataḥ pāvakā naḥ sarasvatīti tisṛṇāmuttamayā paridhāyānantaramukthavīryaṃ vācaṃ me jinvetyevamādikaṃ japati /
7.10.15.[2]	vācaṃ me jinvetyetaiḥ saptabhirvākyaiḥ saptaiva vāyavyāditṛcadevatā āśiṣaḥ prārthyante /

8.1.1.[1]	hotrakaśastrāntaṃ mādhyandinamapi savanaṃ parisamāpya yathā madhyandināya prasṛptāḥ paścimena sadodvāreṇaivamūrdhvaṃ madhyandinātprasarpanti /
8.1.2.[1]	ādau prārambhe tṛtīyasavanasyādityagraheṇa yajñaṃ kurvanti /
8.1.2.[2]	tadyadādityagraheṇa tṛtīyasavanaṃ pratipadyata iti śruteḥ /
8.1.3.[1]	ādityebhyo 'nubrūhītyevamadhvaryuṇokto yadarthaṃ tasya /
8.1.4.[1]	ādityānāmavasā nūtanenetyādityagrahasya puronuvākyā /
8.1.4.[2]	triṣṭubhamādityagrahasya puronuvākyāmanvāheti śruteḥ /
8.1.5.[1]	hotā yakṣadādityānpriyadhāmna ityevamādikaḥ praiṣo bhavati /
8.1.5.[2]	asmai sunvate yajamānāyetyasya vikāreṣūhaḥ /
8.1.6.[1]	ādityāso aditirmādayantāmityetayā yajati /
8.1.6.[2]	triṣṭubhā yajatīti śruteḥ /
8.1.7.[1]	ādityagrahasaṃbandhanīmāhutiṃ hūyamānāṃ hotā nekṣate /
8.1.7.[2]	nāpi grahaśeṣaṃ bhakṣayati /
8.1.8.[1]	lāghavārthaṃ prasaṅgenehaivoktam /
8.1.8.[2]	sāvitragrahe vīkṣaṇamāhuteḥ pratiṣidhyate /
8.1.8.[3]	bhakṣaṇaṃ ca grahaśeṣasya /
8.1.9.[1]	ārbhavākhyena pavamānena stute chandogaiḥ manotādīḍāntaṃ paśukarma kṛtvā /
8.1.9.[2]	tadyathā /
8.1.9.[3]	manotāsūktaṃ pradhānayāgaḥ savasāhomo vanaspatiḥ sviṣṭakṛdiḍāmārjanaṃ cetyetatpaśukarma kṛtvātaḥ purolāśaiḥ savanīyaiścaranti /
8.1.9.[4]	ityayaṃ padārthakramaḥ /
8.1.9.[5]	atha stute pavamāne paśunā carantītyevamādi pradarśitaṃ śrutau /

8.2.1.[3]	tenaiva yajatītyuktam /

8.2.2.[2]	praiṣo yājyā ca pūrvoktā /

9.22.1.[3]	cedagniṃ ceṣyamāṇasya yadṛcchayā yajamānasya dīkṣitasya prāgdīkṣaṇīyāyā ityarthaḥ /
9.22.1.[4]	iṣṭirvakṣyamāṇikā bhavati /
9.22.2.[1]	etāni trīṇi havīṃṣi bhavanti /
9.22.3.[1]	guṇāśaṅkayā saṃdeho mā bhūditi sūtram /
9.22.4.[1]	brahma prajāvadā bhareti puronuvākyā /
9.22.4.[2]	brahma ca te jātavedo namaśceti yājyā /
9.22.4.[3]	kimarthamagnaye brahmavata ityucyate /
9.22.4.[4]	dviprabhṛtiṣu codanānupūrvyeṇeti siddhatvāt /
9.22.4.[5]	ucyate /
9.22.4.[6]	śākhāntareṇa prakṛtaguṇamiṣṭitrayaṃ samāmnātaṃ kvacitkvacidiṣṭidayaṃ /
9.22.4.[7]	tasyārthasya pratipādanārthamevamuktam /
9.22.5.[1]	arcantastvā havāmahe agneḥ kṣatravataḥ puronuvākyā /
9.22.5.[2]	asmā kamagne adhvaraṃ juṣasveti yājyā /
9.22.5.[3]	agne dyumnena jāgṛve ityagneḥ kṣatrabhṛtaḥ puronuvākyā /
9.22.5.[4]	svadasva havyā samiṣo didīhīti yājyā /
9.22.5.[5]	uttarayoriti kṣatravatkṣatrabhṛtoḥ pṛthagapīṣṭirbrahmavata evamiṣṭidayamapi śākhāntare 'stīti jñāyate /
9.22.5.[6]	svaśākhāyāṃ tu trihaviṣkā ekaiveṣṭiḥ /
9.22.6.[1]	iyamiṣṭiḥ saṃnivapanaprayojanā bahūnāṃ ceṣyamāṇānāṃ bhavati /
9.22.6.[2]	te vai dīkṣiṣyamāṇa agnīnsaṃnivapanta ityevamupakramya sarvamāmnātaṃ /
9.22.6.[3]	bahūnāmiti sattriṇo 'bhipretyoktam /
9.22.7.[1]	ekasya cinvataḥ saṃnivapanābhāvāt ukhāsaṃbharaṇaprayojanā dvayameveṣṭirbhavati /
9.22.7.[2]	ukhā viśiṣṭāgnipradhāraṇārthā sthālīviśiṣṭapramāṇā ādhvaryavadharmasamudāyavatī /
9.22.7.[3]	tasyā iṣṭyanantaraṃ upakaraṇāni saṃnivapatītyatra brahmaṇaḥ sākṣyarthaṃ vacanam /
9.23.1.[1]	agnicityāyāmayaṃ cāparo dharmaviśeṣaḥ /
9.23.1.[2]	ādhvaryavādhītena krameṇa prājāpatyaḥ paśubandho bhavati /
9.23.1.[3]	athaitena prājāpatyena paśunā yajanta iti śruteḥ /
9.23.2.[1]	vāyavyo vā paśubandho bhavati śākhāntarāt /
9.23.3.[1]	paśubandho bhavatītyanuvartate /
9.23.3.[2]	vāśabdo vikalpārthaḥ /
9.23.3.[3]	pūrvasūtrādanuvartamāna evocyate /
9.23.3.[4]	kathaṃ nāma agnibhyaḥ kāmāyetyetacchākhāntaroktamupasaṃgṛhyeta /
9.23.4.[1]	puruṣo vaiśyo rājanyo vā /
9.23.4.[2]	ajaḥ chāgaḥ /
9.23.4.[3]	avirmeṣaḥ /
9.23.4.[4]	gauraśvaśca /
9.23.4.[5]	paśuśabdaḥ puruṣe 'pi draṣṭavyaḥ /
9.23.4.[6]	iti pañca paśavaḥ /
9.23.4.[7]	iti prakārapradarśanārthaḥ /
9.23.4.[8]	evaṃprakārā adhvaryuśākhāsu bahavo vikalpāḥ /
9.23.5.[1]	ajo vā eka eva paśurbhavati /
9.23.5.[2]	tūparo viṣāṇarahitaḥ /
9.23.6.[1]	prājāpatye paśau kecidvāyavyaṃ paśupuroḍāśaṃ kurvanti /
9.23.6.[2]	yaddevatyaḥ paśurbhavati taddevatyaṃ paśapuroḍāśamanunirvapatīti prāpte /
9.23.7.[1]	vāyavye paśau eke prājāpatyaṃ paśupuroḍāśaṃ kurvanti /
9.23.8.[1]	agnaye vā kāmāyeti yo 'yamuktastasminneke vaiśvānarīyaṃ paśapuroḍāśaṃ kurvanti /
9.23.9.[1]	prājāpatyasyeti vacanānna sarvatra /
9.23.10.[1]	prājāpatyasyeti vartate /
9.23.11.[1]	ekayā ca daśabhiśca svabhūte /
9.23.11.[2]	rāye nu yaṃ jajñatū rodasīme /
9.23.11.[3]	kuvidaṅga namasā ye vṛdhāsaḥ /
9.23.11.[4]	ityetāḥ puronuvākyā vāyavyasya vapāpuroḍāśapaśūnāṃ /
9.23.11.[5]	pīvoannān rayivṛdhaḥ sumedhāḥ /
9.23.11.[6]	pra yābhiryāsi dāśvāṃsamaccha /
9.23.11.[7]	pra vāyumacchā bṛhatī manīṣetyetāḥ pūrvavat yājyā vāyavyasya /
9.23.11.[8]	niyutvato 'pyetā eva /
9.23.12.[1]	ā te vatso mano yamat tubhyaṃ tā aṅgirastamāgniḥ pareṣu yasya vapāpuroḍāśapaśūnāṃ puronuvākyāḥ /
9.23.12.[2]	vayaṃ te adya rarimā hi kāmaṃ śyāma taṃ kāmamagne tavotī īḍe ca tvā yajamāno havirbhirityetā yājyāḥ /
9.23.12.[3]	agneḥ śuddhasyāpyetā evānyāsaṃbhavāt /
9.23.12.[4]	āgneyasyeti śuddhasyāpyevaṃ nirdeśāt /
9.23.13.[1]	bahuvat bahuvacaneneti yāvat /
9.23.13.[2]	paśunigamāḥ medhamityevamādayaḥ pañcasu paśuṣu kriyamāṇeṣu pṛthivīṃ śarīrāṇīti yāvat /
9.23.13.[3]	prāptamevaitaducyate saṃdehavyudāsārtham /
9.23.14.[1]	ekavacanāntena paśunigamā ata ūrdhvaṃ /
9.23.14.[2]	caturṇāmapsu kāyaprāsanaṃ tato mṛdiṣṭakārthāpaśceti śarīrāṇāṃ viniyogāt /
9.23.14.[3]	ajena yajñasamāptistasmādekavadata ūrdhvam /
9.24.1.[1]	ayaṃ cāparo dharmaviśeṣaḥ sāgnicitye /
9.24.2.[1]	etāni trīṇi havīṃṣi dīkṣaṇīyāyāṃ bhavanti /
9.24.3.[1]	tyānnu kṣatriyāṃ ava iti puronuvākyādityebhyaḥ /
9.24.3.[2]	dhārayanta ādityāso jagatsthā iti yājyā /
9.24.3.[3]	itarayoḥ pūrvopadiṣṭāḥ /
9.24.4.[1]	pañcahaviṣaṃ dīkṣaṇaṇīyāmiṣṭimeke tanvata iti śruteḥ /
9.24.5.[1]	kramārthaṃ vacanaṃ caturthaḥ pañcama iti /
9.24.6.[1]	ekahaviḥ pañcahavirvātithyā kāryā /
9.24.6.[2]	athaitāmātithyāṃ pañcahaviṣamaveṣṭimeke tanvata iti śruteḥ /
9.24.7.[1]	āgneyaindrau puroḍāśau vaiśvadevabārhaspatyau carū vaiṣṇavaśca navakapālaḥ /
9.24.8.[1]	śucimarkairbṛhaspatimiti bārhaspatyasya puronuvākyā /
9.24.8.[2]	taṃ śagmāso aruṣāso aśvā iti yājyā /
9.24.8.[3]	śeṣāṇāṃ pūrvopadiṣṭāḥ /
9.24.9.[1]	citibhyaḥ praṇīyamānābhya ityevamādinā nigadena saṃpreṣito vakṣyamāṇamanuvacanamāha / 10. purīṣyāso agnayaḥ pro tye agnayo 'gniṣu viśvebhiragne agnibhiḥ agne viśvebhiragnibhirityetā ṛco 'nubruvan iṣṭakāḥ praṇīyamānāḥ paścādanusameti /
9.24.9.[2]	athaitā bahvagnīranvāha bahūn hyagnīn praṇayanti tā vai catasro bhavantīti śruteḥ /
9.25.1.[1]	saṃcite 'gnisthale pariṣṭute sāmabhirvakṣyamāṇaṃ karma / 2. prajāpatihṛdayasāmapariṣṭavādanantaraṃ agnyukthamanuśaṃsa iti saṃpreṣito 'gnirjyotirjyotiragnirindro jyotirjyotirindraḥ sūryo jyotirjyotiḥ sūrya ityājyeyastūṣṇīṃśaṃsa uktaḥ /
9.25.1.[2]	yaśca tūṣṇīṃjapaḥ pitā mātariśvetyādistena japena sahokthaṃ śaṃsati /
9.25.1.[3]	āhāvastatra ya uktastaṃ na karoti /
9.25.1.[4]	yattadgrahaṇātsa eva kramaḥ parigṛhyate /
9.25.2.[1]	vaiśvānarāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣitaḥ puronuvākyāmanūcya yājyayā yajati /
9.25.2.[2]	prāptasya punarvacanaṃ parisaṅkhyārthaṃ /
9.25.2.[3]	parisaṅkhyā ca prakṛtiṃ nivartayati / 4. prayājānuyājānvā muktvā śiṣṭānyaṅgāni bhavanti /
9.26.1.[1]	ayaṃ cāparaḥ sāgnicitye viśeṣaḥ /
9.26.1.[2]	agnīṣomīyasya paśoḥ puroḍāśamanugatāni devasūbhyo vakṣyamāṇābhyo devatābhyo devasūsaṃjñikābhyo havīṃṣi bhavanti /
9.26.1.[3]	kābhyaḥ punastābhya ityata āha /
9.26.2.[1]	agnaye gṛhapataya ityevamādibhyo 'ṣṭabhyaḥ saguṇebhyo 'ṣṭau havīṃṣi bhavanti /
9.26.2.[2]	tā vā aṣṭau bhavantīti śruteḥ /
9.26.3.[1]	agnirhotā gṛhapatiḥ sa rājetyagnergṛhapateḥ puronuvākyā /
9.26.3.[2]	havyavāḍagnirajaraḥ pitā na iti yājyā /
9.26.3.[3]	tvaṃ ca soma no vaśa iti somasya vanaspateḥ puronuvākyā /
9.26.3.[4]	brahmā devānāṃ padavīḥ kavīnāmiti yājyā /
9.26.3.[5]	ā viśvadevaṃ na pramiya iti savituḥ satyaprasavasya krameṇa yājyāpuronuvākye /
9.26.3.[6]	yathā no aditiḥ karaditi rudrasya paśupateḥ puronuvākyā /
9.26.3.[7]	upa te stomān paśupā ivākaramiti yājyā /
9.26.3.[8]	bṛhaspate prathamaṃ vāco agramiti bṛhaspatervācaspateḥ puronuvākyā /
9.26.3.[9]	haṃsairiva sakhibhirvāvadabhiriti yājyā /
9.26.3.[10]	indraṃ vayaṃ mahādhana itīndrasya jyeṣṭhasya puronuvākyā /
9.26.3.[11]	uruṃ no lokamanu neṣi vidvāniti yājyā /
9.26.3.[12]	mitrasya carṣaṇīdhṛto mahāṁ āditya iti mitrasya satyasya /
9.26.3.[13]	anadhigacchaṃstalliṅge daivatena tuṣyediti vacanāt /
9.26.3.[14]	imaṃ me varuṇa śrudhīti varuṇasya dharmapateḥ puronuvākyā /
9.26.3.[15]	yatkiṃ cedaṃ varuṇa daivye jana iti yājyā /
9.26.4.[1]	devasūhavirbhyo 'nantarāṇi sarvapṛṣṭhāni havīṃṣi vakṣyamāṇāni bhavanti /
9.27.1.[1]	agnaye vāsantikāya gāyatrāya trivṛte rāthantarāyetyevamādibhyaḥ saguṇebhyo daśa sarvapṛṣṭhāni havīṃṣi /
9.27.1.[2]	tāni vai daśa havīṃṣi bhavantīti śruteḥ /
9.27.2.[1]	arcantastvā havāmahe agnervāsantikādiguṇayuktasya puronuvākyā asmākamadhvaraṃ juṣasveti yājyā /
9.27.2.[2]	indrasya pūrvopadiṣṭe /
9.27.2.[3]	indraṃ vo viśvato mādayasva haribhiriti guṇaviśiṣṭaliṅgānadhigamāt /
9.27.2.[4]	viśve devāsaḥ stīrṇe barhiṣīti vaiśvadevasya pūrvopadiṣṭe /
9.27.2.[5]	ṛtena yāvṛtāvṛdhāviti mitrāvaruṇayoḥ śāradādiguṇayuktayoḥ puronuvākyā pra bāhavā sisṛtaṃ jīvase na iti yājyā /
9.27.2.[6]	bṛhaspaterjuṣasva na iti bṛhaspaterhemantikādiguṇayuktasya puronuvākyā /
9.27.2.[7]	evā pitre viśvadevāya vṛṣṇa iti yājyā /
9.27.2.[8]	anāgaso 'ditaya iti savituḥ śaiśirādiguṇaviśiṣṭasya puronuvākyā vāmamadya savitarvāmam u śva iti yājyā /
9.27.2.[9]	anvadya no anumatirityevamādikānumateḥ puronuvākyā anvidanumate tvamityevamādikā yājyā /
9.27.2.[10]	vaiśvānaro na ūtaya ityagnervaiśvānarasya puronuvākyā pṛṣṭo divīti yājyā /
9.27.2.[11]	ete pūrvopadiṣṭe eva /
9.27.2.[12]	hiraṇyagarbhaḥ samavartatāgra iti kasya puronuvākyā yaḥ prāṇata iti yājyā /
9.27.2.[13]	ete api pūrvopadiṣṭe eva /
9.27.2.[14]	uta tvāmadite mahītyaditerviṣṇupatnyāḥ puronuvākyā mahīmū ṣu mātaramiti yājyā /
9.27.2.[15]	talliṅgānadhigamāt /
9.27.3.[1]	yatra tantre paśuprayuktamaṅgajātaṃ tasminhavīṃṣi codyamānāni pradhānadevatāsaṃbandhena paratantropanipātīni nigamānāvāhanādīnna labhante /
9.27.4.[1]	vapāntamanubandhyāyāḥ karma parisamāpya tvaṣṭṛdevatākena paśunopāṃśu patnīśāle pracaranti /
9.27.4.[2]	nāgniḥ praṇayate /
9.27.4.[3]	atha sunvanti yāvadahaṃ kāmayante /
9.27.4.[4]	athānubandhyasya vapāyāṃ saṃsthitāyāṃ tvāṣṭreṇa paśunetyevamādyupakramya sarvamāmnātam /
9.27.5.[1]	taṃ tvāṣṭraṃ paśuṃ tvāṣṭrapaśukarma paryagnikaraṇāntaṃ kṛtvā utsṛjanti na saṃsthāpayanti /
9.27.5.[2]	paryagnikṛtamutsṛjanti na saṃsthāpayantīti śruteḥ /
9.27.5.[3]	na saṃsthāpayanti vapāyāḥ pūrvaṃ sakalaṃ kurvantītyarthaḥ /
9.27.5.[4]	tata āvāhanaṃ bhavati /
9.27.5.[5]	tathā ca śrutiḥ /
9.27.5.[6]	tadāhuryadete devate āvāhayati tvaṣṭāraṃ ca vanaspatiṃ ca kvāsyaite iṣṭe bhavata iti prayājeṣu vā ete devate yajati tatraivāsyaite iṣṭe bhavata iti /
9.27.6.[1]	vāśabdo vikalpārthaḥ /
9.27.6.[2]	paśudharmaṇā ājyena /
9.27.6.[3]	na pratinidhividhivikāraḥ śabdānāṃ na ca paśudravyasaṃbandhino dharmāḥ kartavyāḥ /

9.27.7.[2]	tvāṣṭrasya paśorājyapakṣe bhavet /
9.28.2.[1]	anumatyādīni pañca havīṃṣi bhavanti /

9.28.3.[1]	anumatyāḥ pūrvopadiṣṭe /
9.28.3.[2]	vibhaktikṛtastu viśeṣaḥ /
9.28.3.[3]	rākāsinīvālībhyāṃ pūrvopadiṣṭāḥ /
9.28.4.[1]	devikāhavibhyo 'nantarāṇi devībhyo havīṃṣi bhavanti /
9.28.4.[2]	cakāraḥ pūrvaiḥ saha samuccayārthaḥ /
9.28.4.[3]	atra haike devībhyo havīṃṣi nirvapanti /
9.28.4.[4]	tathā tāni vai daśa havīṃṣi bhavantīti śruteḥ /
9.28.5.[1]	adbhya ityevamādibhyo daśabhyo daśa devīhavīṃṣyucyante /
9.28.5.[2]	teṣāṃ vakṣyamāṇikā yājyānuvākyāḥ /
9.28.6.[1]	āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva ityapāṃ puronuvākyā /
9.28.6.[2]	yo vo vṛtābhyo akṛṇodu lokamiti yājyā /
9.28.7.[1]	yā oṣadhīḥ pūrvā jātā ityoṣadhīnāṃ puronuvākyā /
9.28.7.[2]	ati viśvāḥ pari ṣṭhā iti yājyā /
9.28.8.[1]	yūyaṃ gāvo medayathā kṛśaṃ ciditi gavāṃ puronuvākyā /
9.28.8.[2]	na tā arvā reṇukakāṭo aśnuta iti yājyā /
9.28.9.[1]	prati ṣyā sūnarī janītyuṣasaḥ puronuvākyā /
9.28.9.[2]	satyā satyebhirmahatī mahadbhiriti yājyā /
9.28.10.[1]	rātrī vyakhyadāyatīti rātreḥ puronuvākyā /
9.28.10.[2]	ye te rātri nṛcakṣasa ityevamādikā yājyā /
9.28.11.[1]	dve te cakre sūrya iti sūryāyāḥ puronuvākyā /
9.28.11.[2]	sukiṃśukaṃ śalmaliṃ viśvarūpamiti yājyā /
9.28.12.[1]	endra yāhi haribhiriti divaḥ puronuvākyā /
9.28.12.[2]	sakhe viṣṇo vitaraṃ vi kramasveti yājyā /
9.28.13.[1]	syonā pṛthivi bhaveti pṛthivyāḥ puronuvākyā /
9.28.13.[2]	balitthā parvatānāmiti yājyā /
9.28.14.[1]	devīṃ vācamajanayanta devā iti vācaḥ puronuvākyā /
9.28.14.[2]	yadvāgvadantyavicetanātīti yājyā /
9.28.15.[1]	mātā rudrāṇāṃ duhitā vasūnāmiti goḥ puronuvākyā /
9.28.15.[2]	vacovidaṃ vācamudīrayantīmiti yājyā /
9.28.16.[1]	devībhyo 'nantaraṃ diśāmaveṣṭīrbhavanti /
9.28.16.[2]	cakāraḥ pūrvaiḥ saha samuccayārthaḥ /
9.28.16.[3]	atra haike diśāmaveṣṭīḥ kurvantīti śruteḥ tathā tāni ve ṣaḍḍhavīṃṣi bhavantīti ca /
9.28.17.[1]	agnaya ityevamādibhyo devatābhyaḥ ṣaḍbhyaḥ ṣaḍḍhavīṃṣi /
9.28.17.[2]	tebhyaḥ pūrvopadiṣṭā yājyāpuronuvākyāḥ /
9.28.18.[1]	ayaṃ cāparaḥ sāgnicitye viśeṣaḥ /
9.28.18.[2]	saṃsthitāyāmudavasānīyāyāmiṣṭau agnihotrahomānte maitrāvaruṇyā payasyayā yāgo bhavati /
9.28.18.[3]	tayā cāniṣṭvāgnicinmaithunaṃ na caret /
9.28.18.[4]	prājāpatyapaśuyāgādārabhyāyaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ /
9.28.18.[5]	tathaiva śatapathaśruteḥ /
9.28.18.[6]	tatra hi prājāpatyapaśuprakaraṇoktaṃ /
9.28.18.[7]	tadāhurnaitena paśaneṣṭvopari śayīta na māṃsamaśnīyānna mithunamupeyāt pūrvadīkṣā vā eva paśuḥ anavaklṛptaṃ vai tadyaddīkṣita upari śayīta yanmāṃsamaśnīyādyanmithunamupeyāditi /
9.28.18.[8]	na tvevaiṣā dīkṣā naiva hi mekhalāsti na kṛṣṇājinamiṣṭakāṃ vā etāṃ kurute tasmādu kāmamevopari śayītaitadu sarvamannaṃ yadete paśavastadasyātrāsamārabdhaṃ bhavati tadyāni kāni cāmadhuno 'śanāni teṣāmasya sarveṣāṃ kāmāśanaṃ yadi labheta /
9.28.18.[9]	mithunaṃ tu nopeyātpurā maitrāvaruṇyai payasyāyā iti /

10.6.2.[2]	jagatprātaḥsavano hyeṣa tryaha iti śruteḥ / 3. agniṃ taṃ manye yo vasuriti samūḍhapakṣe ājyaṃ kāryam /
10.6.3.[1]	tasyāgniṃ taṃ manya ityetasya prathamāyai śaṃsanārthaṃ prakṛtivatpadaṃ avagṛhya padamavagṛhya avasya dve avagṛhya avasya /
10.6.3.[2]	ekena praṇauti /
10.6.3.[3]	evametāṃ satrirvacanāṃ śastvā tataḥ /

10.6.5.[1]	śrutyanukaraṇārthaṃ vacanamabṛhatīnāṃ coddhāraḥ pakṣe /
10.6.6.[1]	ā no yajñamiti dve /
10.6.6.[2]	ā no vāyo mahe tana ityekā /
10.6.6.[3]	ityayaṃ vāyavyastṛcaḥ / 8. ā vāṃ sahasraṃ haraya ityaindravāyavastṛcaḥ /
10.6.6.[4]	tisro 'pi gāyatryaḥ bārhatākhyastu cchatrinyāyena / 9. ṛdhagitthā sa martya ityete dve /
10.6.6.[5]	pra mitrāya prāryamṇa ityekā maitrāvaruṇo 'yaṃ tṛcaḥ / 10. āśvino 'yaṃ tṛcaḥ / 11. tṛco 'yamaindraḥ / 12. devaṃdevaṃ vo 'vase devaṃdevamabhiṣṭaya ityevamādiko vaiśvadevastṛcaḥ /
10.6.6.[6]	yastu prāthamyādāśaṅkyate devaṃdevaṃ vo 'vasa indramindraṃ gṛṇīṣaṇītyayaṃ na bārhato nāpi vaiśvadevaḥ /
10.6.6.[7]	tatra kecidāhuranyo 'pyevamādiko bārhataśca vaiśvadevaśca śākhāntare 'sti /
10.6.6.[8]	tannivṛttyarthaṃ viśeṣaṇam / 13. iyamadadādrabhasamṛṇacyutamiti sārasvatastṛcaḥ /
10.6.6.[9]	etānyuktāni praugatṛcāni /
10.6.6.[10]	purorucastu nityāḥ /

10.6.8.[1]	yatpāñcajanyayā viśeti marutvatīyasya pratipaditi śruteḥ /
10.6.9.[1]	itthā hi soma inmada iti mahatpāṃktamiti śruteḥ sūktaṃ /
10.6.9.[2]	avitāsi sunvato vṛktabarhiṣa iti ṣaṭpadā iti śruteḥ /
10.6.9.[3]	marutvāṁ indra vṛṣabho raṇāyeti vijñātatraiṣṭubhamiti śruteḥ /
10.6.9.[4]	ayaṃ ha yena vā idamiti tisraḥ /
10.6.9.[5]	evamekastṛcaḥ trīṇi ca pūrvāṇi sūktānīti marutvatīyaṃ /

10.6.13.[1]	yā sā paṅktiruttamā tasyā uttame pāde pañca padāni purīṣākhyāni nivicchaṃsaṃ śaṃset /
10.6.13.[2]	na praṇavamantarā kuryādityarthaḥ /

10.6.14.[5]	sa iti sādṛśyārthe śabdanirdeśāt /
10.6.15.[1]	yadindra nāhuṣīṣveti sāmnaḥ pragātha iti śruteḥ /
10.6.16.[1]	indro madāya vāvṛdha iti madvatpāṃktaṃ predaṃ brahma vṛtratūryeṣvāvitheti ṣaṭpadāḥ /
10.6.16.[2]	abhūreko rayipate rayīṇāmiti vijñātatraiṣṭubhaṃ savanadharaṇaṃ tamindraṃ vājayāmasīti tisraḥ /

10.6.18.[1]	udu ṣya devaḥ savitā damūnā iti tṛcaṃ sāvitraṃ /

10.6.18.[3]	ṛbhurvibhvā vāja indro no acchetyārbhavaṃ /

10.6.18.[5]	iti vaiśvadeve vikāro 'nyaprākṛtam /
10.6.19.[1]	haviṣpāntamajaraṃ svarvidīti vaiśvānarīyaṃ /

10.7.7.[11]	prātaḥsavane prasthitānāmetā yājyāḥ /
10.7.8.[1]	tubhyaṃ hinvāno vasiṣṭha gā apa iti ṣaḍṛcayoḥ sūktayorekaikā hotrādīnāmṛtupraiṣādūrdhvaṃ yājyā bhavati /
10.7.8.[2]	nityā pūrvānṛtuyājān kṛtvā gārtsamadairyajantīti śruteḥ /

10.8.14.[2]	tasya dve uttame pariśiṣya ye yajñena dakṣiṇayā samaktā ityetaṃ nārāśaṃsaṃ samāvapatīti śruteḥ /
10.8.14.[3]	pariśiṣṭe idamitthetyasya sūktasya ye mukte tasminkrame śaṃsatīti vaiśvadeve vikāro 'nyatprākṛtam /
10.8.15.[1]	ahaśca kṛṣṇamahararjunaṃ ceti vaiśvānarīyamiti śruteḥ / 26. prayajyavo maruto bhrājadṛṣṭaya iti mārutamiti śruteḥ / 27. imaṃ stomamarhate jātavedasa iti jātavedasīyamiti śruteḥ /

10.8.19.[2]	caturthe 'hani yanmārutamuktaṃ ka īṃ vyaktā iti tasyānte samāptāvityarthaḥ /
10.8.19.[3]	pra yantu vājāstaviṣībhiragnaya iti tisraḥ karoti śaṃsatītyarthaḥ /
10.8.19.[4]	pra yantu vājāstaviṣībhiragnaya iti tisro 'dhikāḥ samūḍhā iti śruteḥ /
10.8.20.[1]	caturthasya samūḍha iti vartate /
10.8.20.[2]	vasuṃ na citramahasaṃ gṛṇīṣa ityetaccaturthe 'hani samūḍhe jātavedasīyaṃ bhavati /
10.8.20.[3]	huve vaḥ sudyotmānamiti nivartate /
10.8.21.[1]	vaiyūḍhikātṣaḍahātsāmūḍhike yo viśeṣaḥ sa uktaḥ /
10.8.21.[2]	parokṣapṛṣṭhādiṣu tu cchandogavaśena stotriyānurūpānsāmapragāthāṃśca kuryāt /
10.8.21.[3]	tatra hi sāmaparokṣe eteṣveva stotriyeṣu anyāni sāmāni kramāt sāmaparokṣe 'nurūpeṣvanyāni tatrānurūpe 'pi vairāje kriyamāṇe nyūṅkho bhavatyeva /
10.8.21.[4]	vairājasyeti sāmāśrayatvāt /
10.8.21.[5]	yadi punarvirāṭsu sāmāntaraṃ bhavati tato na nyūṅkhaḥ /
10.8.21.[6]	na hi vairājaṃ tatsthānamanyūṅkhanāyeti śruteḥ /
10.8.21.[7]	śākvaraṃ tu nānyāsṛkṣu na śakvarīṣvanyasāmeti samākhyānāt /
10.8.21.[8]	bṛhadrathantaramitare /
10.8.21.[9]	atha kasmādanvahaṃ bṛhatkriyata iti śruteḥ /
10.8.21.[10]	daśame vāhani svayonau rathantaraṃ /
10.8.21.[11]	upāyapṛṣṭha āparkyapṛṣṭhe tanūṣpṛṣṭhe brahmasāmāni cchandoruṭstome vyūḍhāḥ stomā iti cchandogavārttā /
10.8.22.[1]	uktānāṃ ṣaḍahānāṃ ye viśeṣā uktāstadvyatiriktamanyattulyaṃ samūḍhena /
10.8.22.[2]	tataśca samūḍha eṣāṃ prakṛtiḥ /
10.8.22.[3]	ukthamukhīyayostu nyūṅkho bhavatyeva hotuḥ /
10.8.22.[4]	yasmācchandogavaśena stotriyānurūpānsāmapragāthāṃśceti vacanaṃ /
10.8.22.[5]	śrutyarthavādaścānugṛhīto bhavati /
10.8.22.[6]	atha kasmāccaturthe 'hani nyūṅkhayatītyevamādikaḥ /
10.8.23.[1]	viśvajidapi parokṣapṛṣṭho bṛhadrathantarapṛṣṭha upāṅkyapṛṣṭha āparkyapṛṣṭhastanūpṛṣṭaśchandoruṭstoma ityetaiḥ prakārairbhavati /
10.8.23.[2]	tasyāpi tathaiva bhavati yathā ṣaḍahasya cchandogavaśena stotriyānurūpakriyā sāmapragāthakriyā ca /
10.8.23.[3]	agniṃ nara ityagniṣṭomasāmnaḥ stotriyānurūpāvityetadasaṃyujya vidhīyamānatvātsarvatra sādhāraṇam /
10.8.23.[4]	bṛhadrathantarapṛṣṭhayoryadi bhavati bṛhatpratyakṣapṛṣṭhastatrāpi tvaṃ hi caitavadyaśa ityetadājyaṃ bhavati /
10.8.23.[5]	ubhayasāmāpi bṛhatpṛṣṭho bhavatyevātha kasmādanvahaṃ bṛhatkriyata iti liṅgāt /
10.8.23.[6]	tanūpṛṣṭhasya sāmapragāthāṃśchastvā yonī parokṣapṛṣṭhe /
10.8.23.[7]	na kaṇvabṛhadrathantarayoryonī /
10.8.23.[8]	svasti no mimītāmiti ca tisro 'nte vaiśvadevānāṃ karotītyetatsamānamanyatsamūḍheneti vacanādviśvajityapi sarveṣu bhavati /
10.8.23.[9]	parokṣapṛṣṭhe 'pi na hotuḥ pratiśilpakriyā hotrakāṇāṃ tatrādhikārāt /
10.9.1.[1]	madhye daśarātra iti prakṛtam /
10.9.1.[2]	tasya pṛṣṭhyaṣaḍaha uktaḥ /
10.9.1.[3]	trayaśca cchandomā vaktavyāḥ /
10.9.1.[4]	tatra tāvacchāndomikaṃ prathamamahardaśarātrasya saptamaṃ taducyate /
10.9.1.[5]	caturviṃśastomaṃ sarvamahaḥ /
10.9.1.[6]	hotrakāṇāṃ stomātiśaṃsanārthaṃ vacanaṃ /
10.9.1.[7]	bṛhatpṛṣṭhamiti svaśrutyabhiprāyaḥ /
10.9.1.[8]	bṛhadrathantarapṛṣṭhe 'pi daśarātre yukṣu bṛhṛdayukṣu rathantaramevaṃ prāpte 'pyasya saptamasyāhno bṛhṛtpṛṣṭhataiva vacanāt /
10.9.2.[1]	pra vaḥ śakrāya bhānave bharadhvamityājyamiti śruteḥ /
10.9.3.[1]	vakṣyamāṇakaḥ /
10.9.4.[1]	pra vīrayā śucayo dadrire vāmiti vāyavyamiti śruteḥ tṛcam / 5. te satyena manasā dīdhyānā ityaindravāyavastṛcaḥ / 6. udvāṃ cakṣurvaruṇa supratīkamiti maitrāvaruṇamiti śruteḥ / 7. ā gomatā nāsatyā rathenetyāśvinam / 8. ā no deva śavasā yāhi śuṣminnityaindram / 9. pra vo yajñeṣu devayanto arcanniti vaiśvadevam / 10. pra kṣodasā dhāyasā sasra eṣeti sārasvatam /
10.9.4.[2]	ityetāni praugatṛcāni /
10.9.5.[1]	ye pārṣṭhikasya prathamasya tryahasya pratipadanucarāḥ sabrāhmaṇaspatyāścoktāste chandomeṣu bhavanti /
10.9.5.[2]	svarasāmānaśca vakṣyante teṣu ca ta evaṃ bhavanti /
10.9.5.[3]	abhiplave ca ṣaḍahe āvṛttyā ta evaṃ bhavanti /
10.9.5.[4]	evamatidiṣṭānāṃ viśeṣaviniyoga ucyate /
10.9.6.[1]	pārṣṭhikātprathamādahaḥ prathamasya cchāndomikasyāhno bhavanti /
10.9.7.[1]	dvitīyātpārṣṭhikāt dvitīyasya cchāndomikasyāhno bhavanti /
10.9.8.[1]	tṛtīyātpārṣṭhikāt pratipadanucarāḥ sabrāhmaṇaspatyāstṛtīyasya cchāndomikasyāhno bhavanti /
10.9.9.[1]	evameveti pāṭhakrameṇa tryahasya pūrvasyābhiplavikasya pārṣṭhikāḥ pratipadanucarāḥ sabrāhmaṇaspatyāḥ prathamatryahoktā bhavanti /
10.9.10.[1]	ābhiplavikasyeti vartate /
10.9.10.[2]	yena krameṇa pūrvasyābhiplavikasya tryahasya tenaiva krameṇottarasyāpi /
10.9.10.[3]	ye tryahasya prathamasya pratipadanucarāḥ sabrāhmaṇaspatyāste chandomeṣvevamādiyattadornirdeśaṃ kurvannaikāhikānāṃ pakṣe prāptiṃ darśayati /
10.9.11.[1]	itthaṃ chāndomikenaiva krameṇa svarasāmnāmapi pārṣṭhikaprathamatryahoktāḥ pratipadanucarāḥ sabrāhmaṇaspatyāḥ /
10.9.11.[2]	svarasāmabhyaḥ śastrāṇītyatra prākṛtavikalpārthamevamityatirekavacanaṃ /
10.9.11.[3]	vyutkramādyupadeśaḥ chandomānāmabhiplavasya ca vaiśvadevasāhacaryārthaṃ /
10.9.12.[1]	kayā śubhā savayasaḥ sanīḍāḥ /
10.9.12.[2]	tyaṃ su meṣaṃ mahayā svarvidamiti traiṣṭubhajāgate sūkte marutvatīyam evameva śrutatvāt /
10.9.13.[1]	tamu ṣṭuhi yo abhibhūtyojā abhi tyaṃ meṣaṃ puruhūtamṛgmiyamiti traiṣṭubhajāgate sūkte ubhe abhivatī /
10.9.13.[2]	tadrāthantaraṃ rūpaṃ dvedve sūkte niṣkevalyamarutvatīyayoḥ śasyete iti śrutatvāt /
10.9.14.[1]	yadyu kaṇvarathantaraṃ kuryurnāsya yonimanuśaṃset iti śruteḥ /
10.9.15.[1]	ye prathamayoḥ prathamadvitīyayorityarthaḥ /
10.9.15.[2]	ahnoḥ pārṣṭhikayorevaṃnāmatvāt /
10.9.15.[3]	prathame 'hani chāndomike prathamātpārṣṭhikāt /
10.9.15.[4]	dvitīye dvitīyāt /
10.9.15.[5]	tṛtīye prathamāt /
10.9.15.[6]	rāthantaraṃ śastramiti śrutiliṅgāt /
10.9.15.[7]	evamābhiplavike prathame prathamātpārṣṭhikāt dvitīye dvitīyāt tṛtīye prathamādityādi jñeyam /
10.9.16.[1]	tatsaviturvareṇyamiti sāvitraṃ tṛcaṃ sūktaṃ /
10.9.16.[2]	pretāṃ yajñasya śaṃbhuveti dyāvāpṛthivīyaṃ tṛcaṃ sūktaṃ /
10.9.16.[3]	ayaṃ devāya janmana ityārbhavaṃ tṛcaṃ sūktaṃ /
10.9.16.[4]	tṛcagrahaṇaṇat /
10.9.16.[5]	ṛjunītī no varuṇa iti pañcarcaṃ vaiśvadevaṃ /
10.9.16.[6]	ā yāhi vanasā saheti dvyṛcaṃ sūktaṃ /
10.9.16.[7]	sūktasaṅkhyāvacanādāmnānācca /
10.9.16.[8]	chandovicitau ca pitubhṛto na tantumidityudāhṛtatvāt catuṣpadā /
10.9.16.[9]	omāmaścarṣaṇīdhṛta iti tisraḥ /
10.9.16.[10]	ityeṣa vaiśvadeve vikāraḥ /
10.9.17.[1]	vaiśvānaro na ūtaya iti kalpajā punarādheyapaṭhitā /
10.9.17.[2]	vaiśvānaro na ā gamadityevamādike gāyatryāviha paṭhite /
10.9.17.[3]	etattṛcaṃ vaiśvānarīyaṃ sūktaṃ /
10.9.17.[4]	pra yadvastriṣṭubhamiti pañcadaśa nava veti mārutaṃ /
10.9.17.[5]	arcantastvā havāmaha iti jātavedasīyaṃ /
10.9.17.[6]	ityāgnimārute vikāraḥ /
10.10.1.[1]	daśarātrasyāṣṭamamahaścatuścatvāriṃśastomaṃ /
10.10.1.[2]	stomasaṅkhyā hotrakāṇāmekayā dvābhyāṃ vā stomamatiśaṃsatītyevaṃ prayojanā /
10.10.1.[3]	rathantarapṛṣṭhamiti svaśrutiprakāśakam /
10.10.2.[1]	agniṃ vo devamagnibhiḥ sajoṣā ityājyamiti śruteḥ /
10.10.3.[1]	vakṣyamāṇakaḥ /
10.10.4.[1]	kuvidaṅga namasā ye vṛdhāsa ityete prathamatṛtīye dve vāyavyasya tṛcasya / 5. ā vāyo bhūṣa śucipā upa na ityekā /
10.10.4.[2]	pūrvābhyāṃ saha samuccayārthaścakāraḥ / 6. yāvattarastanvo yāvadoja ityaindravāyavaḥ / 7. prati vāṃ sūra udite sūktairiti maitrāvaruṇamiti śruteḥ / 8. apa svasuruṣaso nagjihīta ityāśvinamiti śruteḥ / 9. ayaṃ soma indra tubhyaṃ sunva ityaindramiti śruteḥ / 10. pra brahmāṇo aṅgiraso nakṣanteti vaiśvadevamiti śruteḥ / 11. uta syā naḥ sarasvatī juṣāṇeti sārasvatamiti śruteḥ /
10.10.4.[3]	ityetāni praugatṛcāni /
10.10.5.[1]	mahāṁ indro nṛvadā carṣaṇiprā iti traiṣṭubhānāṃ prathamaṃ marutvatīyānāmityevamārabhya sarvamāmnātaṃ śrutau /
10.10.5.[2]	kva sya vīraḥ ko apaśyadindramityatra sūkte bhadramidaṃ ruśamā agne akranniti catasraḥ sarvatroddhartavyāḥ /
10.10.5.[3]	śrutyantarāt /
10.10.5.[4]	narastuterdaivatāsaṃdehācca /
10.10.6.[1]	tvaṃ mahāṁ indra tubhyaṃ ha kṣā iti traiṣṭubhānāṃ prathamaṃ niṣkevalyānāmityevamanukramya śrutau sarvamāmnātam /
10.10.7.[1]	caturṛcametatsāvitram / 15. mahī dyauḥ pṛthivī cana iti tṛcaṃ sūktaṃ dyāvāpṛthivīyam /
10.10.7.[2]	yuvānā pitarā punarityārbhavam / 16. devānāmidavo mahaditi navarcaṃ vaiśvadevamiti śruteḥ / 17. imā nu kaṃ bhuvanā sīṣadhāmeti dvipadā iti śruteḥ / 18. viśve devā ṛtāvṛdha ityetāstisraḥ /
10.10.7.[3]	sūktavivṛddhāvantye nividasminprathame tvāhāvo devānāmidavo mahadityasmin /
10.10.7.[4]	iti vaiśvadeve vikāraḥ /
10.10.8.[1]	dve iha paṭhite kalpaje tṛtīyā cāpyupadiṣṭābhyuddraṣṭāyāmiti vaiśvānarīyam / 20 . mārutametacchruteḥ / 21. dūtaṃ vo viśvavedasamiti jātavedasīyam /
10.10.8.[2]	ityāgnimārute vikāraḥ /
10.11.1.[1]	daśarātrasya navamamaharvakṣyamāṇaṃ tadaṣṭācatvāriṃśastomaṃ /
10.11.1.[2]	hotrakāṇāṃ stomātiśaṃsanārthā stomasaṅkhyā bṛhatpṛṣṭhamiti svaśrutyabhiprāyaḥ /
10.11.2.[1]	aganma mahā namasā yaviṣṭhaṃ somasya mā tavasaṃ vakṣyama ityete ubhe tadājyamiti śruteḥ /
10.11.3.[1]	aganma mahā namasā yaviṣṭhaṃ somasya mā tavasaṃ vakṣyama ityetayoryatpūrvaṃ tadeva kevalamājyaṃ bhavati /
10.11.3.[2]	tathā ca śruteḥ /
10.11.4.[1]	vakṣyamāṇakaḥ /
10.11.5.[1]	ā vāyo bhūṣa śucipā upa na iti pañcakasya sūktasya prathamātṛtīye dve ṛcau uttamā caivaṃ vāyavyastṛcaḥ / 6. ā vāyo bhūṣetyasyaiva sūktasya dvitīyācaturthyāvṛcau /
10.11.5.[2]	arvanto na śravaso bhikṣamāṇā iti ca tṛtīyetyevamendravāyavastṛcaḥ / 7. divi kṣayantā rajasaḥ pṛthivyāmiti maitrāvaruṇamiti śruteḥ / 8. ā viśvavārāśvinā gataṃ na ityāśvinamiti śruteḥ / 9. indraṃ naro nemadhitā havanta ityaindramiti śruteḥ / 10. ūrdhvo agniḥ sumatiṃ vasvo aśrediti vaiśvadevamiti śruteḥ / 11. pra kṣodasā dhāyasā satra eṣeti sārasvatamiti śruteḥ /
10.11.5.[3]	ityetāni praugatṛcāni /
10.11.6.[1]	tryaryamā manuṣo devatātetyevamanukramya pañca sūktāni marutvatīye śasyanta uttame chandoma iti śruteḥ /
10.11.7.[1]	ā satyo yātu maghavāṁ ṛjīṣīti traiṣṭubhānāṃ prathamaṃ niṣkevalyānāmityevamādyanukramya ṣaḍantato niṣkevalya iti vacanāt ṣaṭsūktaṃ niṣkevalyam /
10.11.8.[1]	abhi tvā deva savitariti sāvitraṃ tṛcaṃ sūktaṃ /
10.11.8.[2]	pra vāṃ mahi dyavī abhīti dyāvāpṛthivīyaṃ tṛcaṃ sūktam / 15. indra iṣe dadātu na ityekā /
10.11.8.[3]	te no ratnāni dhattaneti dve ityārbhavamiti śruteḥ / 16. agnirukthe purohita ityevamādīni pañca sūktāni /
10.11.8.[4]	saha tṛtīyena sūktena teṣāṃ tṛtīyaṃ vā kaśyapa iti savikalpena / 17. ye triṃśati trayaspara ityetatsūktamupottamāmuddhṛtya / 18. sūktanivṛttyarthamekāgrahaṇam / 19. ā śarma parvatānāmityetāścatasraḥ / 20. babhrureko viṣuṇaḥ sūnaro yuveti caitatsūktaṃ bhavati /
10.11.8.[5]	vāśabdaḥ pūrveṇa saha vikalpārthaḥ /
10.11.8.[6]	manupravarhavacanādubhayapakṣe 'pi bhāradvājastṛco bhavati /
10.11.8.[7]	ubhayoḥ pañcayostulyatvāt /
10.11.8.[8]	ye triṃśatītyupottamāmuddhṛtya na hi vo astyarbhaka ityekā śarmeti catasro babhrureka iti vā manupravarho /
10.11.8.[9]	manoḥ pravarha iti vṛhū udyamana ityasya prapūrvasyājantasya rūpaṃ /
10.11.8.[10]	prakarṣodyatasāra ityarthaḥ /
10.11.8.[11]	yasmāccāyaṃ sārastasmānna kiṃciduddhartavyam /

10.11.8.[13]	iti vaiśvadeve vikāraḥ /
10.11.8.[14]	abhi tvā devetyata ārabhya bhāradvājatṛcāvadhikaḥ /
10.11.9.[1]	divi pṛṣṭha ityevamādike dve kalpaje /
10.11.9.[2]	tṛtīyā ca sārvakāmikyāṃ /
10.11.9.[3]	ityetattṛcaṃ vaiśvānarīyam / 23. maruto yasya hi kṣaya iti mārutamiti śruteḥ / 24. agnirhotā purohita iti jātavedasīyamiti śruteḥ / 25. vikāra iti vākyaśeṣaḥ /
10.11.9.[4]	vyūḍhapakṣe chandomānāṃ yadvaktavyaṃ taduktaṃ /
10.11.9.[5]	samūḍhapakṣa idānīmāha /
10.11.10.[1]	vyūḍhapakṣe yāni tryahasya prathamasya prātaḥsavanatṛtīyasavanānyuktāni tāni samūḍhapakṣe chandomānāmiti diśyante /
10.11.10.[2]	kiṃcānyat /
10.11.11.[1]	yāni ca niṣkevalyamarutvatīyayoḥ chandomagatayorjāgatāni vyūḍhe 'bhihitāni tāni samūḍhapakṣa utsṛjati /
10.11.11.[2]	caśabdāt /
10.11.12.[1]	sa yo vṛṣā vṛṣṇyebhiḥ samokā ityetāḥ pañcadaśa kayāśubhīyādūrdhvaṃ bhavanti /
10.11.13.[1]	yo jāta eva prathamo manasvānityetatsūktaṃ tamuṣṭuhīyādūrdhvaṃ bhavati /
10.11.14.[1]	bṛhadrathantarapṛṣṭho daśarātraḥ pākṣiko 'sti /
10.11.14.[2]	tasminkriyamāṇe sarve chandomamadhyandinā hoturdiṣūktā bhavanti /
10.11.14.[3]	sarva iti vacanāt saṃghātaprayuktāḥ naikaikatvena prayujyamānāḥ /
10.12.1.[1]	daśamamaharidānīṃ vaktavyaṃ /
10.12.1.[2]	tadevaṃsaṃjñakaṃ na vivaktavyamityavivākyaṃ /
10.12.1.[3]	kecittu manyante na nāmadheyamityetat saṃvyavahārābhāvāt /
10.12.1.[4]	avivākyamiti guṇavidhānametat /

10.12.1.[6]	caturviṃśastomaṃ /

10.12.3.[1]	mānasaṃ stotraṃ trikaṃ bhavati /

10.12.5.[1]	yadi cetkasyacicchaṃsataḥ pratibhāhāniḥ syāttato 'nyo 'viniyuktastadupadeśārthaṃ svādhyāyavadanubrūyāt /
10.12.5.[2]	nandati ha vai yajño viduṣāgacchatā yato 'samṛddhaṃ bhaviṣyatyayaṃ me tatsamardhayiṣyatīti /
10.12.5.[3]	yadi kaścitpramatta upahanyādyastadadhīyāt sa taṃ deśaṃ pārśvataḥ svādhyāyamadhīyīteti śruteḥ /
10.12.6.[1]	uddhṛtyānuṣṭubhaṃ chando yatprākṛtamitareṣāmanuṣṭubvivarjitānāṃ chandasāmanuṣṭupsaṃpadaṃ saṃpādya pañcadaśaṃ sahasraṃ kāryamekasmintsavanīye /
