10.12.6.[255]	tā no rāsanrātiṣāco vasūnīti catasraḥ /
10.12.6.[256]	ṣaṣṭhī cānobhadrīyasya /
10.12.6.[257]	bhadraṃ karṇebhiriti ca /
10.12.6.[258]	viśve devāḥ śṛṇutemaṃ havaṃ me /
10.12.6.[259]	ghṛtaṃ mimikṣe ghṛtamasya yoniḥ /
10.12.6.[260]	tvaṃ soma pitṛbhiḥ saṃvidānaḥ bhavā mitro na śevyo ghṛtāsutiḥ /
10.12.6.[261]	aibhiragne sarathaṃ pāhyarvāṅ /
10.12.6.[262]	ā te pitarmarutāṃ sumnametu /
10.12.6.[263]	aprayucchannaprayucchadbhiragne /
10.12.6.[264]	uta no 'hirbudhnyaḥ śṛṇotu /
10.12.6.[265]	uta gnā vyantu devapatnīḥ /
10.12.6.[266]	paitryastisraḥ /
10.12.6.[267]	svāduṣkilīyāstisraḥ /
10.12.6.[268]	yayorojasā skabhitā rajāṃsi /
10.12.6.[269]	viṣṇornu kaṃ vīryāṇi pra vocam /
10.12.6.[270]	evā na indro maghavā virapśīti tisraḥ /
10.12.6.[271]	tiṣṭhā su kaṃ maghavanmā parā gāḥ /
10.12.6.[272]	atipraiṣasya puronuvākyā /
10.12.6.[273]	parā yāhi maghavannā ca yāhīti pañca patnīsaṃyājeṣviti triṣṭubhaḥ /
10.12.6.[274]	atha jagatyaḥ /
10.12.6.[275]	ekā aponaptrīye /
10.12.6.[276]	ṣoḍaśābhiṣave /
10.12.6.[277]	pinvantyapa ityekā /
10.12.6.[278]	dve haviṣyapaṃktyāṃ /
10.12.6.[279]	ṣaṭ prasthitayājyāḥ /
10.12.6.[280]	sāvitragrahasya ca yājyā /
10.12.6.[281]	catasraḥ sāvitre sūkte /
10.12.6.[282]	pañca dyāvāpṛthivīye /
10.12.6.[283]	catasra ārbhave /
10.12.6.[284]	yebhyo mātetyekā /
10.12.6.[285]	ṣaḍānobhadrīye /
10.12.6.[286]	vaiśvānarāya pṛthupājasa iti trayodaśa /
10.12.6.[287]	pratvakṣasaḥ pratavaso virapśina iti ṣaṭ /
10.12.6.[288]	pra tavyasīṃ navyasīṃ dhītimagnaya iti sapta /
10.12.6.[289]	devānāṃ patnīrityekā /
10.12.6.[290]	rākāmahamiti dve /
10.12.6.[291]	tantuṃ tanvannityekā /
10.12.6.[292]	agne marudbhiḥ śubhayadbhirityekā /
10.12.6.[293]	yunajmi te brahmaṇā keśinetyekā /
10.12.6.[294]	punaśca devānāṃ patnīriti /
10.12.6.[295]	atha dvipadāḥ /
10.12.6.[296]	dve niṣkevalye /
10.12.6.[297]	ekaikā hotrakāṇāṃ śastreṣu /
10.12.6.[298]	ekaviṃśatirvaiśvadeva iti /
10.12.6.[299]	athāṣṭayaḥ /
10.12.6.[300]	trikadrukeṣu mahiṣo yavāśiraṃ tuviśuṣma ityeṣā triḥ /
10.12.6.[301]	abhi tyaṃ devaṃ savitāramoṇyorityeṣā tririti /
10.12.6.[302]	atha śakvaryau /
10.12.6.[303]	tacchaṃyorā vṛṇīmaha iti śakvarī dviḥ prayujyate /
10.12.6.[304]	evametadyathopanyastadṛḍhīkaraṇāya saṃpattyarthaiḥ ślokairanūdyate /
10.12.6.[305]	śatadvayaṃ sapañcāśamapa ityataḥ param /
10.12.6.[306]	gāyatramuṣṇihaścātra ṣoḍaśāṣṭau virājakāḥ // 1 //
10.12.6.[307]	bṛhatyo 'pi bhavantyatra catvāriṃśattribhiḥ saha /
10.12.6.[308]	ekaṣaṣṭyadhikaṃ viddhi triṣṭubhāṃ ca śatadvayam // 2 //
10.12.6.[309]	paṅktayaḥ ṣoḍaśāśītirjagatīnāṃ suniścitā /
10.12.6.[310]	dvipadā viṃśatiḥ ṣaṭ ca dve śakvaryau ṣaḍaṣṭayaḥ // 3 //
10.12.6.[311]	uktā evaṃ pṛthagbhūtāḥ kriyante 'nuṣṭubho yadā /
10.12.6.[312]	tadānena prakāreṇānyathā vā yathecchayā // 4 //
10.12.6.[313]	śakvaryau bṛhatīraṣṭīrgāyatrīṇāṃ gaṇe kṣipet /
10.12.6.[314]	anuṣṭubhastathaitāḥ syustriṣṭubekātiricyate // 5 //
10.12.6.[315]	traiṣṭubhātpūrvasaṃkhyātādekaṣaṣṭācchatadvayāt /
10.12.6.[316]	aṣṭānavatiranveti caturakṣaravarjitā // 6 //
10.12.6.[317]	caturakṣarahīnāni śatāni trīṇyanuṣṭubhām /
10.12.6.[318]	saṃpannānyūnaṣaṣṭāni triṣṭupsvapi na saṃśayaḥ // 7 //
10.12.6.[319]	uṣṇihaśca virājaśca paṅktayaścaikadhā kṛtāḥ /
10.12.6.[320]	dvicatvāriṃśadetāḥ syuḥ śruteranyā anuṣṭubhaḥ // 8 //
10.12.6.[321]	jagatīnāmaśītiryā tadviṃśatiśataṃ bhavet /
10.12.6.[322]	saṃpadā ṣoḍaśa jñeyā dvipadotthā anuṣṭubhaḥ // 9 //
10.12.6.[323]	saptāśītāni saptaiva pūrvoktāni hyanuṣṭubhām /
10.12.6.[324]	dvādaśāgne tamityaṣṭeḥ saṃpannāḥ śruticoditāḥ // 10 //
10.12.6.[325]	gāyatryādigaṇāstriṣṭuppādaśca dvipadotthitaḥ /
10.12.6.[326]	caturakṣaramādāya pūrayettriṣṭubhaṃ tataḥ // 11 //
10.12.6.[327]	śeṣairanuṣṭubhaṃ kuryādevamaṣṭau śatāni tu /
10.12.6.[328]	ṣoḍaśaivātiriktāni akṣarāṇīha yojayet // 12 //
10.12.6.[329]	triṣṭubhaśca dvirukteyaṃ dvādaśākṣarahīnikā /
10.12.6.[330]	tubhyaṃ ścotanti tisṛbhirevaṃ ṣoḍaśa yojayet // 13 //
10.12.6.[331]	sahasrametacchrutyuktaṃ pūrṇaṃ pañcadaśādhikam /
10.12.6.[332]	sahaprātaranuvākaṃ saṃpadānuṣṭubhāmiha // 14 //
10.12.6.[333]	agnisvāminoktā atraiva ślokā likhyante /
10.12.6.[334]	athānyānuṣṭubuddhāraḥ sa hi sarvatra coditaḥ /
10.12.6.[335]	na yatharthyāpriyābhāve noddhāraḥ syādanuṣṭubhām //
10.12.6.[336]	prajākāmavaśādyāgaḥ sinīvālyāḥ kriyeta cet /
10.12.6.[337]	nātra tatra tu kartavye sve khalvasyā anuṣṭubhau //
10.12.6.[338]	uddhṛtyānuṣṭubhaṃ yasmācchandasāṃ saṃpaducyate /
10.12.6.[339]	śatātirātra ukthyādestasmānnānuṣṭubhastyajet //
10.12.6.[340]	ucchrayasveti na tyājyā saptānāṃ codanārambhāt /
10.12.6.[341]	ye vṛkṣāsa iti tveṣā vyaktavyā tadvicāritam //
10.12.6.[342]	devo 'gnistvabhikṛtireṣā pṛthaktvādvigaṇyatām /
10.12.6.[343]	iti syānnetaraḥ śuddhastulyapratyāyako hyayam //
10.12.6.[344]	sarvā dāśatayīṣvetā uttarāstu subheṣajaḥ /
10.12.6.[345]	anena vyapadeśena ṛkṣvapyasyā atulyatā //
10.12.6.[346]	trikadrukeṣvabhi tyaṃ ca śaṃyorvāke tathaiva ca /
10.12.6.[347]	dvāvaticchandasāṃ vargāvativargottarāśrayāt //
10.12.6.[348]	atulyā iti cettatra pratipatsaṃpadaśruteḥ /
10.12.6.[349]	sarvārtho vetaracchando virājastena na tyajet //
10.12.6.[350]	virāḍanuṣṭubhoraikyādudvriyeranvirājo 'pi /
10.12.6.[351]	saṃpatsyācchandasāmatra savanīyaviśeṣaṇāt //
10.12.6.[352]	atiriktakriyāyāṃ hi saṃpannaiveti cedbhavet /
10.12.6.[353]	ekasminniti vārambhādadhikeṣu tvanādaraḥ //
10.12.6.[354]	ekasminniti satyetadvākyaṃ syādavivakṣitam /
10.12.6.[355]	iti syāttatra yenoktamanārambho bhavedyasya //
10.12.6.[356]	ājyabhāgau vikalpena śaṃyorvākaśca yaḥ paraḥ /
10.12.6.[357]	brahmasāmaparāt svā ca sinīvālī ca rākā ca //
10.12.6.[358]	tathā paśapuroḍāśaḥ sviṣṭakṛtaśca yo bhavet /
10.12.6.[359]	ekāhena ca vidyante tāyamānasya rūpāṇi //
10.12.6.[360]	pūrvakārivaśātkarma svaśāstre yadi kalpitam /
10.12.6.[361]	kriyetābhyadhikaṃ kiñcidūnaṃ vāpi kadā cana //
10.12.6.[362]	svaśāstravihitaṃ vā syāt pūrvakārī na cet kuryāt /
10.12.6.[363]	saṃpat tatrāpi saṃpādyā tadārambhaḥ prayojanam //
10.12.6.[364]	athārghyāprīprayogena kratuyājyā vikalpane /
10.12.6.[365]	na cettathāpi pūryeta saṃpattatrāvapediha //
10.12.6.[366]	yathākāmī prakaraṇe jñāpakaṃ parameketi /
10.12.6.[367]	ūrdhvaṃ cokthyamukhīyāyā āvāpo 'trāpi coditaḥ //
10.12.6.[368]	athavonnīyamāneṣu sūktānāṃ parimāṇataḥ /
10.12.6.[369]	śruteḥ saṃpatsu saṃpādyā śrutidṛṣṭā kriyā yadi //
10.12.6.[370]	adṛṣṭaṃ tu yadasmākaṃ kriyetābhyadhikaṃ rucitam /
10.12.6.[371]	saṃpattatra na saṃpādyā jñāpakaṃ paśavo adhikāḥ //
10.12.6.[372]	vājinaṃ ca na saṃkhyeyaṃ taddhyasmākamacoditam /
10.12.6.[373]	payasyāṃgamidaṃ hīti syādiyaṃ kasya cinmatiḥ //
10.12.6.[374]	sākamedheṣu taccāpi pratiṣedhānna yujyate /
10.12.6.[375]	gaṇyate cātiriktokthe samākhyā hitayostathā //
10.12.6.[376]	atyantaṃ caiva bhedātsyātsaṃpadā viṣame hite /
10.12.6.[377]	somātirekaśastraṃ ca vai tābhyāmuktakāraṇam //
10.12.6.[378]	śastraṃ kalaśabhede yadbhāvabhede ca yadbhavet /
10.12.6.[379]	saṃpattatrāpi saṃpādyā tatraitannāsti kāraṇam //
10.12.6.[380]	somārambhāttrivṛtstomena saṃpādyā bhavetsaṃpat /
10.12.6.[381]	kāryastvanuṣṭubuddhāraḥ sūtrārambhātpunaḥpunaḥ //
10.12.6.[382]	uktārambho viśeṣārtho na teṣāṃ sāsti codanā /
10.12.6.[383]	kuryurityupadeśāddhi tasmātteṣu na saṃpatsyāt //
10.12.6.[384]	anuṣṭupsaṃpadamata ucyamānāṃ nibodhata /
10.12.6.[385]	dve prātaranuvāke tu śate pañcadaśādhike /
10.12.6.[386]	jagatyekāponaptrīye triṣṭubhāṃ viṃśatistisraḥ /
10.12.6.[387]	gāyatryo yasya pītveti na saṃkhyā nigadā gaṇyāḥ //
10.12.6.[388]	saṃpadānuṣṭubho hyeṣā ekaviṃśatsaṃpādikā /
10.12.6.[389]	yatparivyayaṇīyādi bhavanīyāntamatra tu //
10.12.6.[390]	ājyabhāgāvasaṃkhyāya saṃkhyāyaikaṃ paśuṃ tathā /
10.12.6.[391]	āpriyastriṣṭubhaḥ saṃkhyaṃ sarveṣāṃ saṃpadastathā //
10.12.6.[392]	prajākāmavadāprīṇāṃ nārāśaṃsyapi vāsiṣṭhī /
10.12.6.[393]	gāyatrī vā bhavenmatvā saṃpadgaṇyā ṛco 'tra tu //
10.12.6.[394]	satobṛhatyastisro 'tra dvāviṃśatiśca triṣṭubhaḥ /
10.12.6.[395]	tubhyaṃ ścotanti vāpyeṣā virāṭrūpāṣṭakottamā //
10.12.6.[396]	catvāriṃśacca tisraśca gāyatryaḥ syuranuṣṭubhām /
10.12.6.[397]	aṣṭāvaṣṭistu saṃpannāḥ ṣoḍaśākṣaravarjitāḥ //
10.12.6.[398]	dvidevatyādi cājyāt prāgṛtuyācyā ṛco na tu /
10.12.6.[399]	bṛhatyo nava gāyatryaḥ catvāriṃśacca pañca ca //
10.12.6.[400]	ekā satobṛhatyatra saṃpadānuṣṭubhaḥ pañca /
10.12.6.[401]	catvāriṃśacca tāḥ sārdhaṃ caturbhiḥ syurihākṣaraiḥ //
10.12.6.[402]	saṃpadānuṣṭubhaścājye daśa tisraśca niścitāḥ /
10.12.6.[403]	sayājye prauge ca syuḥ saṃpadā daśa sapta ca //
10.12.6.[404]	hotrājyeṣu sayājyeṣu ṣaṣṭiradhyardhayā vinā /
10.12.6.[405]	savane 'nuṣṭubhāṃ saṃpaccatvāriṃśacca pañca ca //
10.12.6.[406]	śatāni pañca catvāryakṣarāṇi ca viṃśatiḥ /
10.12.6.[407]	grāvastotre tu gāyatryastrayastriṃśattathoṣṇihaḥ //
10.12.6.[408]	tisraḥ satobṛhatyekā jagatyaḥ ṣoḍaśaiva tu /
10.12.6.[409]	triṣṭubhaḥ sapta saṃpannā dviṣaṣṭiḥ syātsapādikā //
10.12.6.[410]	dadhigharmādiśastrāt prāk syāccetpaśapuroḍāśaḥ /
10.12.6.[411]	tatsviṣṭakṛtpṛthaktve tu triṃśatsaikātra triṣṭubhām //
10.12.6.[412]	gāyatryekā ca saṃpannāścatvāriṃśadanuṣṭubhaḥ /
10.12.6.[413]	adhikā tisṛbhirjñeyā akṣarāṇi ca dvādaśa //
10.12.6.[414]	ekā marutvatīye tu sayājye jagatyastisraḥ /
10.12.6.[415]	aṣṭayaḥ pañca gāyatryaścatasraḥ kakubhastathā //
10.12.6.[416]	bṛhatyaḥ satobṛhatyastriṣṭubhaḥ ṣoḍaśaiva tu /
10.12.6.[417]	catvāriṃśaccatasraśca saṃpannāḥ pādavarjitāḥ //
10.12.6.[418]	niṣkevalye sayājye tu gāyatryo 'ṣṭau virāḍekā /
10.12.6.[419]	tisraḥ satobṛhatyo 'tra bṛhatyastisra eva ca //
10.12.6.[420]	triṣṭubho 'ṣṭādaśa jñeyā dvipade dve navoṣṇihaḥ /
10.12.6.[421]	catvāriṃśatsahāṣṭābhiḥ saṃpannāḥ syuranuṣṭubhām //
10.12.6.[422]	maitrāvaruṇaśastre tu sayājye dvipadaikikā /
10.12.6.[423]	ekā satobṛhatyatra triṣṭubho daśa sapta ca //
10.12.6.[424]	triṣṭubhastrirvirāṭsthānānmukhyātsyānnavako nava /
10.12.6.[425]	bṛhatyaḥ saṃpadā tu syāccatvāriṃśadvinoṣṇihaḥ //
10.12.6.[426]	brāhmaṇacchaṃsinaḥ śastre bārhate stotriye kṛte /
10.12.6.[427]	ekā satobṛhatyatra sayājye dvipadā tathā //
10.12.6.[428]	bṛhatyo nava vijñeyāḥ triṣṭubhaścaikaviṃśatiḥ /
10.12.6.[429]	saṃpadānuṣṭubhastvetāścatvāriṃśatsahoṣṇihā //
10.12.6.[430]	acchāvākasya triṣṭubhaḥ śastra ekānnaviṃśatiḥ /
10.12.6.[431]	ekā satobṛhatyekā sayājye dvipadā tathā //
10.12.6.[432]	bṛhatyo 'nuṣṭubhāṃ triṃśatsāṣṭā sacaturakṣarā /
10.12.6.[433]	savane 'nuṣṭubhāṃ saṃpacchatāni trīṇi pañca ca //
10.12.6.[434]	jñeyāni daśabhiḥ sārdhamakṣarāṇi ca ṣoḍaśa /
10.12.6.[435]	syācchastrādvaiśvadevātprāgyadādityagrahādi tu //
10.12.6.[436]	jagatyo 'tra nava jñeyāścatvāriṃśacca triṣṭubhaḥ /
10.12.6.[437]	abhūddeva iti triṣṭubevamanyasyāśucimatā //
10.12.6.[438]	saṃpadānuṣṭubho hyetā aṣṭāṣaṣṭiḥ sahārdhena /
10.12.6.[439]	vaiśvadevādi saṃkhyāya parījyā sāgnimārutam //
10.12.6.[440]	triṣṭubho viṃśatistatra jagatyaścaikaviṃśatiḥ /
10.12.6.[441]	ṣaṭ gāyatryo 'ṣṭayastisro dvipadāścaikaviṃśatiḥ //
10.12.6.[442]	saṃpannānāmaśītiḥ ṣaṭviṃśatyakṣarasaṃyutā /
10.12.6.[443]	ekatriṃśajjagatyaḥ syuḥ sayājye tvāgnimārute //
10.12.6.[444]	yāste rāke sumataya eṣopajagatī smṛtā /
10.12.6.[445]	triṣṭubho 'ṣṭādaśa jñeyāstisraścākṣarapaṅktayaḥ //
10.12.6.[446]	virājaḥ ṣaṭ ca gāyatryastisraḥ syuḥ saṃpadā tviha /
10.12.6.[447]	anuṣṭubhāṃ tryaśītiḥ syādadhikāṣṭābhirakṣaraiḥ //
10.12.6.[448]	śaṃyorvākādi śaṃyvantaṃ śaṃyuḥ syuḥ syādihottaraḥ /
10.12.6.[449]	sinīvālī ca rākā ca kriyeyātāṃ na cediha /
10.12.6.[450]	gāyatryau dve jagatyekā śakvaryau dve tathaiva ca /
10.12.6.[451]	upatriṣṭup ca vijñeyāyaṃ yajña itīyamṛk //
10.12.6.[452]	triṣṭubho 'ṣṭau tu saṃpannāḥ syuḥ ṣoḍaśabhirakṣaraiḥ /
10.12.6.[453]	adhikā daśabhiḥ sārdhaṃ sadā jñeyā anuṣṭubhaḥ //
10.12.6.[454]	savane 'nuṣṭubhāṃ saṃpacchatānyardhatṛtīyāni /
10.12.6.[455]	dve caivātrāpare jñeye caturakṣaravarjite //
10.12.6.[456]	yāste rāke jagatī vā jñeyā triṣṭubathāpi vā /
10.12.6.[457]	evaṃ saṃpāditā saṃpadyuktā brāhmaṇakalpayoḥ //
10.12.7.[1]	upaprayanto nava sa hi yo mānuṣā yugeti catasraḥ kasta uṣaḥ iti tisro yāvayadveṣasaṃ tveti catasro 'śvinā yajvarīriṣa iti tisra ā me havaṃ naveti /
10.12.8.[1]	agniṃ naro dīdhitibhiraraṇyoriti tṛcamāgneye /
10.12.8.[2]	prati ṣyā sunarī janītyuṣasye /
10.12.8.[3]	ā śubhrā yātamaśvinā svaśvetyāśvine /
10.12.9.[1]	āpo revatīḥ kṣayathā hi vasva iti triḥ samasya yadviyutā sasminnūdhanniti pañcāganma maheti tisra upo ruruce ṣaṭ prati stomebhiriti tṛcaṃ /
10.12.9.[2]	ā bhātyagniruṣasāmanīkamiti dve upa tyā vahnī gamato viśaṃ na iti dve iti caturviṃśatiṃ triṣṭubho 'nubrūyāt /
10.12.10.[1]	vediṣada iti sapta janasya gopā iti ṣaṭ etā u tyā iti tisraḥ triścinno adyeti catasraḥ va svidadya katamāsvaśvineti catasra ityetāścaturviṃśatiṃ jagatīranubrūyāt /
10.12.11.[1]	enā vo agniṃ namaseti trayaḥ pragāthāḥ /
10.12.11.[2]	ayamagniḥ suvīryasyeti trayaḥ pragāthāḥ /

10.21.12.[3]	uttarasya havirdhānasyādho'kṣaṃ yajamānāḥ sarpanti /
10.21.13.[1]	uttareṇāgāraṃ yajñasyānusaṃcaranta iti śruteḥ /
10.21.14.[1]	yuvaṃ tamindrāparvatā puroyudhetyetāmaticchandasaṃ japanto 'dho'kṣaṃ sarpanti /
10.21.14.[2]	uttareṇa vā gacchanto 'kṣavelāyāṃ taduddeśa ityarthaḥ /
10.21.14.[3]	tato'greṇa havirdhāne samupaviśya /
10.21.14.[4]	saṃśabdādekapradeśa āsīnāḥ kāmāndhyāyante yatkāmāḥ sattriṇaḥ /
10.21.15.[1]	ye bahukāmāḥ sattriṇo 'nekakāmāḥ pṛthakkāmā ityarthaḥ /
10.21.15.[2]	bhūrbhuvaḥ svarityetāste vyāhṛtīrna tu pratīkagrahaṇāt suprajā ityevamādikaṃ mantram /
10.21.16.[1]	te yajanto yajamānāste vā ṛtvijaḥ asattre /
10.21.16.[2]	śākhāntaropadeśāt /
10.21.16.[3]	te prāñca udañca utkramya vācaṃ vihvayante vispaṣṭamuccairāhvayanta ityarthaḥ /
10.21.16.[4]	katham /
10.21.16.[5]	vāgaitu vāgupaitu vāgupa maitu vāgiti /
10.21.17.[1]	subrahmaṇyāpratīkaṃ subrahmaṇyomiti trirupāṃśūktvā vācaṃ visṛjante ye pūrva vāgyatāḥ /
10.21.18.[1]	kecinmānasamaharantaraṃ vadanti /
10.21.18.[2]	kecidudayanīyānte /
10.21.18.[3]	apare daśamāharaṅgaṃ /
10.21.18.[4]	tadabhiprāyaṃ sūtrametat /
10.21.18.[5]	tannirākaraṇāyedamārabhyate 'nantaraṃ sūtram /
10.21.19.[1]	kālavāda eṣaḥ /
10.21.19.[2]	yo 'yaṃ purā patnīsaṃyājebhyaḥ saṃsthāpya veti /
10.21.19.[3]	yathā divi devanādīnāmabhiṣecanīyamadhye paṭhitānāmapi nābhiṣecanīyāṅgatvaṃ /
10.21.19.[4]	kālamātravādo 'sminnavadhau /
10.21.19.[5]	paṣṭhauhīṃ dīvyati rājanyaṃ jinātītyevamādayo 'bhiṣecanīyamadhye 'pi kriyamāṇā rājasūyāṅgaṃ evaṃ sattrotthānaṃ daśame 'pyahani kriyamāṇaṃ dvādaśāhāṅgamiti /
10.21.19.[6]	ato vāśabdaḥ parābhiprāyanivṛttyarthaḥ /
